# How It Works - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Context Connectors

How It Works

On this page

*   [Architecture](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#architecture)
    
*   [Data Flow](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#data-flow)
    
*   [Indexing](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#indexing)
    
*   [Searching](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#searching)
    
*   [File Reading (MCP/Agent)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#file-reading-mcp%2Fagent)
    
*   [Incremental Updates](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#incremental-updates)
    

Context Connectors is a pipeline that indexes your code and content for semantic search. Here’s how the pieces fit together.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#architecture)

Architecture
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Content flows through five components:

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#)

Source

Connect to your content: GitHub, GitLab, BitBucket, or website

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#)

Indexer

Discover files, filter, chunk, and send to Context Engine for embedding

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#)

Store

Persist index state (local filesystem or S3) for incremental updates

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#)

Context Engine

Augment’s semantic search backend stores embeddings and handles queries

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#)

Client

Query via CLI, MCP server, or your own application

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#data-flow)

Data Flow
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#indexing)

Indexing

When you run `ctxc index`, here’s what happens:

1.  **Discover** - Source connector lists all files (respects `.gitignore`)
2.  **Filter** - Skip binary files, large files, excluded patterns
3.  **Hash** - Compute file hashes to detect changes
4.  **Diff** - Compare with stored state to find new/modified/deleted files
5.  **Index** - Send changed files to Context Engine for embedding
6.  **Save** - Store new state for next incremental run

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#searching)

Searching

When you run `ctxc search` or query via MCP:

1.  **Query** - User submits natural language query
2.  **Embed** - Context Engine converts query to vector
3.  **Match** - Find semantically similar code chunks
4.  **Return** - Results with file paths, line numbers, and snippets

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#file-reading-mcp/agent)

File Reading (MCP/Agent)

When an agent needs full file content (not just search snippets):

1.  **Request** - Agent requests file by path
2.  **Fetch** - MCP server reads from original source (filesystem or Git API)
3.  **Return** - Full file content returned to agent

This is why MCP servers need source credentials (e.g., `GITHUB_TOKEN`) - they read files on demand from the original source, not from the index.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/how-it-works#incremental-updates)

Incremental Updates
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Context Connectors tracks file state to avoid re-indexing unchanged files:

| Scenario | What Happens |
| --- | --- |
| File unchanged | Skipped (hash matches) |
| File modified | Re-indexed |
| File deleted | Removed from index |
| New file | Added to index |

State is stored in your chosen store:

*   **Local filesystem** - Platform-specific directory (e.g., `~/.local/share/context-connectors` on Linux)
*   **S3** - `s3://bucket/index-name/` prefix

This makes subsequent runs fast - only changed files are processed.

[Custom Client](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-client)
[CLI Reference](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/cli-reference)

⌘I

# Overview - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Context Connectors

Overview

On this page

*   [Getting Started](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview#getting-started)
    
*   [Quickstart Recipes](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview#quickstart-recipes)
    
*   [Advanced Recipes](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview#advanced-recipes)
    
*   [Documentation](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview#documentation)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

**Build indexes** from Git repos (GitHub, GitLab, BitBucket) or documentation websites. Index code, documentation, runbooks, schemas, configs, and more. Use DirectContext in the Context Engine SDK for custom sources. **Store indexes** on your local filesystem for fast & simple access, or in S3 for persistent storage in production apps. **Search indexes** via interactive agent, MCP for AI integrations, CLI for quick searches, or DirectContext in the Context Engine SDK for custom implementations.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview#getting-started)

Getting Started
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New to Context Connectors?** Here’s a suggested path:

1.  **Index and search** → [Index and Search Code](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos)
     (3 min)
2.  **Connect an agent** → [Local MCP Server](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration)
     (3 min)
3.  **Build an app** → [Store Indexes in S3](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3)
     (5 min)
4.  **Automate updates** → [GitHub Actions Auto-Indexing](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing)
     (5 min)

Or jump directly to any recipe below.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview#quickstart-recipes)

# Auto-Index with Webhooks - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Quickstart Recipes

Auto-Index with Webhooks

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#prerequisites)
    
*   [Steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#steps)
    
*   [1\. Create a Vercel project](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#1-create-a-vercel-project)
    
*   [2\. Create the webhook handler](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#2-create-the-webhook-handler)
    
*   [3\. Set environment variables in Vercel](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#3-set-environment-variables-in-vercel)
    
*   [4\. Deploy](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#4-deploy)
    
*   [5\. Configure GitHub webhook](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#5-configure-github-webhook)
    
*   [6\. Test it](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#6-test-it)
    
*   [Done!](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#done)
    
*   [Also Works With](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#also-works-with)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   A Vercel account (or Express server)
*   Augment API credentials
*   AWS credentials + S3 bucket
*   A GitHub repo you control

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#steps)

Steps
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#1-create-a-vercel-project)

1\. Create a Vercel project

Copy

Ask AI

    npx create-next-app@latest my-webhook --typescript --app
    cd my-webhook
    npm install @augmentcode/context-connectors @aws-sdk/client-s3
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#2-create-the-webhook-handler)

2\. Create the webhook handler

Create `app/api/webhook/route.ts`:

Copy

Ask AI

    import { createVercelHandler } from "@augmentcode/context-connectors/integrations/vercel";
    import { S3Store } from "@augmentcode/context-connectors/stores";
    
    const store = new S3Store({ bucket: process.env.INDEX_BUCKET! });
    
    export const POST = createVercelHandler({
      store,
      secret: process.env.GITHUB_WEBHOOK_SECRET!,
      shouldIndex: (event) => event.ref === "refs/heads/main",
    });
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#3-set-environment-variables-in-vercel)

3\. Set environment variables in Vercel

Copy

Ask AI

    AUGMENT_API_TOKEN=your-token
    AUGMENT_API_URL=https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/
    GITHUB_WEBHOOK_SECRET=your-secret
    INDEX_BUCKET=my-indexes
    AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=your-key
    AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY=your-secret
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#4-deploy)

4\. Deploy

Copy

Ask AI

    npx vercel --prod
    

Note the URL (e.g., `https://my-webhook.vercel.app`).

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#5-configure-github-webhook)

5\. Configure GitHub webhook

1.  Go to your repo → Settings → Webhooks → Add webhook
2.  Payload URL: `https://my-webhook.vercel.app/api/webhook`
3.  Content type: `application/json`
4.  Secret: same as `GITHUB_WEBHOOK_SECRET`
5.  Events: Just the push event
6.  Click “Add webhook”

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#6-test-it)

6\. Test it

Push a commit to main. Check Vercel logs for:

Copy

Ask AI

    Indexed myorg/myrepo: 142 files indexed
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#done)

Done!
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your index updates automatically on every push to main.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook#also-works-with)

Also Works With
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Instead of… | Try… |
| --- | --- |
| Vercel | Express: `createExpressHandler()` from `integrations/express` |
| Vercel | Any framework: `createGitHubWebhookHandler()` + `verifyWebhookSignature()` |
| Main branch only | Customize `shouldIndex` to match any branch pattern |
| S3 storage | `FilesystemStore` for local/self-hosted setups |

[GitHub Actions Auto-Indexing](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing)
[Custom Indexer](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-indexer)

Context Services

Overview

On this page

*   [What Are Context Services?](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview#what-are-context-services)
    
*   [Context Engine MCP](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview#context-engine-mcp)

*   [Context Connectors](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview#context-connectors)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview#what-are-context-services)

What Are Context Services?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Context Services provide high-quality semantic search to AI agents and applications. Whether you’re building custom agents or integrating with existing AI tools, Context Services give you access to Augment’s world-class context engine.

[Context Engine MCP\
------------------\
\
Plug Context Engine into any agent via the Model Context Protocol](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview)
[Context Engine SDK\
------------------\
\
Build context-aware custom agents or apps using our TypeScript or Python SDK](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview)
[Context Connectors\
------------------\
\
Index any source and make it searchable via CLI, MCP, or HTTP](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview#context-engine-mcp)

Context Engine MCP

Plug Context Engine into any agent, such as Claude Code, Codex, Gemini CLI, and more via the Model Context Protocol (MCP). **Perfect for:**

*   Using Augment’s context in your favorite AI tools
*   Enriching any coding agent or AI with state-of-the-art codebase semantic search

[Get started with MCP →](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview#context-engine-sdk)

Context Engine SDK

Build context-aware custom agents or apps using our TypeScript or Python SDK. The SDK provides **FileSystem Context** to index local directories or **Direct Context** to index files from any source. **Perfect for:**

*   Building custom AI agents with codebase understanding
*   Creating applications that need to understand codebase, documentation, specifications, runbooks, and other text sources
*   Achieving state-of-the-art context quality in AI-powered code review, security scanning, failure analysis, migrations, and more …

[Get started with the SDK →](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview#context-connectors)

Context Connectors

An open-source library built on the Context Engine SDK that makes diverse sources searchable across agents and apps. Index code, documentation, runbooks, schemas, and configs from GitHub, GitLab, BitBucket, websites, or local filesystem. Store indexes locally or in S3. Search via CLI, interactive agent, or MCP server. **Perfect for:**

*   Indexing repositories without cloning them locally
*   Building applications with persistent indexes stored in S3
*   Auto-indexing on every push via webhooks
*   Indexing documentation websites

[Get started with Context Connectors →](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview)

[Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/using-augment/vim-completions)
[Context Engine MCP](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview)

⌘I

Custom Client

On this page

*   [Basic Search Client](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-client#basic-search-client)

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

Build custom search clients to load indexes and provide search functionality for web apps, CLIs, or serverless functions.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-client#basic-search-client)

Basic Search Client
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   TypeScript
    
*   Python
    

Copy

Ask AI

    import { SearchClient, FilesystemStore } from "@augmentcode/context-connectors";
    
    // Create a search client
    const client = new SearchClient({
      store: new FilesystemStore({ basePath: "./indexes" }),
      indexName: "my-docs",
    });
    
    // Initialize (loads index from store)
    await client.initialize();
    
    // Search
    const { results } = await client.search("authentication");
    console.log(results);
    
    // Ask a question about the search results
    const answer = await client.searchAndAsk(
      "authentication",
      "How does auth work?"
    );
    console.log(answer);
    

Copy

Ask AI

    from auggie_sdk.context import DirectContext
    import os
    
    class SearchClient:
        def __init__(self, index_name: str, store_path: str = None):
            self.index_name = index_name
            self.store_path = store_path
            self.context = None
    
        def initialize(self):
            # Load search-optimized state (smaller, no file list)
            search_file = os.path.join(self.store_path, self.index_name, 'search.json')
            self.context = DirectContext.import_from_file(search_file)
    
        def search(self, query: str):
            return self.context.search(query)
    
        def ask(self, search_query: str, prompt: str = None):
            return self.context.search_and_ask(search_query, prompt)
    
    # Usage
    client = SearchClient('my-docs', store_path='./indexes')
    client.initialize()
    results = client.search('authentication')
    answer = client.ask('authentication', 'How does auth work?')
    

Search clients load `search.json` which is optimized for search operations. The full `state.json` file is only needed by indexers for incremental updates.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-client#web-application)

Web Application
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   TypeScript (Express)
    
*   Python (Flask)
    

Copy

Ask AI

    import express from "express";
    import { SearchClient, FilesystemStore } from "@augmentcode/context-connectors";
    
    const app = express();
    app.use(express.json());
    
    // Initialize client at startup
    const client = new SearchClient({
      store: new FilesystemStore(),
      indexName: "my-docs",
    });
    await client.initialize();
    
    app.post("/api/search", async (req, res) => {
      const { query } = req.body;
      const { results } = await client.search(query);
      res.json({ results });
    });
    
    app.post("/api/ask", async (req, res) => {
      const { query, question } = req.body;
      const answer = await client.searchAndAsk(query, question);
      res.json({ answer });
    });
    
    app.listen(3000);
    

Copy

Ask AI

    from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
    
    app = Flask(__name__)
    client = SearchClient('my-docs')
    client.initialize()
    
    @app.post('/api/search')
    def search():
        query = request.json['query']
        results = client.search(query)
        return jsonify({'results': results})
    
    @app.post('/api/ask')
    def ask():
        query = request.json['query']
        prompt = request.json.get('prompt')
        answer = client.ask(query, prompt)
        return jsonify({'answer': answer})
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-client#cli-client)

CLI Client
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   TypeScript
    
*   Python
    

Copy

Ask AI

    import { program } from "commander";
    import { SearchClient, FilesystemStore } from "@augmentcode/context-connectors";
    
    program
      .command("search <query>")
      .option("-i, --index <name>", "Index name", "my-project")
      .action(async (query, options) => {
        const client = new SearchClient({
          store: new FilesystemStore(),
          indexName: options.index,
        });
        await client.initialize();
        const { results } = await client.search(query);
        console.log(results);
      });
    
    program
      .command("ask <query>")
      .option("-i, --index <name>", "Index name", "my-project")
      .option("-q, --question <question>", "Question to ask")
      .action(async (query, options) => {
        const client = new SearchClient({
          store: new FilesystemStore(),
          indexName: options.index,
        });
        await client.initialize();
        const answer = await client.searchAndAsk(query, options.question);
        console.log(answer);
      });
    
    program.parse();
    

Copy

Ask AI

    import click
    
    @click.group()
    def cli():
        pass
    
    @cli.command()
    @click.argument('query')
    @click.option('--index', default='my-project')
    def search(query, index):
        client = SearchClient(index)
        client.initialize()
        print(client.search(query))
    
    @cli.command()
    @click.argument('query')
    @click.option('--index', default='my-project')
    @click.option('--prompt')
    def ask(query, index, prompt):
        client = SearchClient(index)
        client.initialize()
        print(client.ask(query, prompt))
    
    if __name__ == '__main__':
        cli()
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-client#serverless-function)

Serverless Function
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   TypeScript (AWS Lambda)
    
*   Python (AWS Lambda)
    

Copy

Ask AI

    import { SearchClient, S3Store } from "@augmentcode/context-connectors";
    
    let client: SearchClient | null = null;
    
    async function getClient() {
      if (!client) {
        client = new SearchClient({
          store: new S3Store({ bucket: "my-indexes" }),
          indexName: "my-docs",
        });
        await client.initialize();
      }
      return client;
    }
    
    export async function handler(event: any) {
      const body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");
      const { query } = body;
    
      const client = await getClient();
      const { results } = await client.search(query);
    
      return {
        statusCode: 200,
        body: JSON.stringify({ results }),
      };
    }
    

Copy

Ask AI

    import json
    
    client = None
    
    def get_client():
        global client
        if client is None:
            client = SearchClient('my-docs')
            client.initialize()
        return client
    
    def lambda_handler(event, context):
        body = json.loads(event.get('body', '{}'))
        query = body.get('query')
    
        client = get_client()
        results = client.search(query)
    
        return {
            'statusCode': 200,
            'body': json.dumps({'results': results})
        }

# Custom Indexer - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-indexer#content-area)

Advanced Recipes

Custom Indexer

On this page

*   [Basic Example](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-indexer#basic-example)
    
*   [Data Source Examples](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-indexer#data-source-examples)
    
*   [Automation](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-indexer#automation)
    
*   [Next Steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-indexer#next-steps)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

Build a custom indexer to fetch content from any source (API, database, CMS) and index it with DirectContext.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-indexer#basic-example)

Basic Example
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   TypeScript
    
*   Python
    

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Indexer, FilesystemStore } from "@augmentcode/context-connectors";
    import type { Source, FileEntry, FileChanges, SourceMetadata, FileInfo } from "@augmentcode/context-connectors";
    
    // Implement the Source interface for your data source
    class ApiSource implements Source {
      readonly type = "custom" as const;
    
      async fetchAll(): Promise<FileEntry[]> {
        // Replace with your actual data source (API, database, CMS, etc.)
        const response = await fetch("https://api.example.com/docs");
        const docs = await response.json();
        return docs.map((doc: any) => ({
          path: doc.path,
          contents: doc.content,
        }));
      }
    
      async fetchChanges(previous: SourceMetadata): Promise<FileChanges | null> {
        // Return null to always do full re-index
        // Or implement incremental updates based on your data source
        return null;
      }
    
      async getMetadata(): Promise<SourceMetadata> {
        return {
          type: "custom",
          identifier: "api-docs",
          ref: new Date().toISOString(),
          syncedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        };
      }
    
      async listFiles(directory?: string): Promise<FileInfo[]> {
        const files = await this.fetchAll();
        return files.map(f => ({ path: f.path, type: "file" as const }));
      }
    
      async readFile(path: string): Promise<string | null> {
        const files = await this.fetchAll();
        return files.find(f => f.path === path)?.contents ?? null;
      }
    }
    
    // Usage
    const source = new ApiSource();
    const store = new FilesystemStore({ basePath: "./indexes" });
    const indexer = new Indexer();
    
    const result = await indexer.index(source, store, "my-docs");
    console.log(`Indexed ${result.filesIndexed} files (${result.type})`);
    

Copy

Ask AI

    from auggie_sdk.context import DirectContext, File
    import json
    import os
    from pathlib import Path
    
    class CustomIndexer:
        def __init__(self, store_path: str = None):
            self.store_path = store_path
    
        def fetch_files(self):
            """Fetch from your data source (API, database, CMS, etc.)"""
            # Replace with your actual data source
            return [\
                File(path='docs/intro.md', contents='# Introduction\n...'),\
                File(path='docs/api.md', contents='# API Reference\n...'),\
            ]
    
        def index(self, index_name: str):
            index_dir = os.path.join(self.store_path, index_name)
            state_file = os.path.join(index_dir, 'state.json')
    
            # Load existing or create new context
            if os.path.exists(state_file):
                context = DirectContext.import_from_file(state_file)
            else:
                context = DirectContext.create()
    
            # Fetch and index files
            files = self.fetch_files()
    
            # Handle incremental updates
            indexed_paths = set(context.get_indexed_paths())
            current_paths = {f.path for f in files}
            paths_to_remove = [p for p in indexed_paths if p not in current_paths]
    
            if paths_to_remove:
                context.remove_from_index(paths_to_remove)
    
            context.add_to_index(files)
    
            # Export both full and search-only states
            full_state = context.export(mode='full')
            search_state = context.export(mode='search-only')
    
            # Save both files
            Path(index_dir).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    
            with open(os.path.join(index_dir, 'state.json'), 'w') as f:
                json.dump(full_state, f, indent=2)
    
            with open(os.path.join(index_dir, 'search.json'), 'w') as f:
                json.dump(search_state, f, indent=2)
    
    # Usage
    indexer = CustomIndexer(store_path='./indexes')
    indexer.index('my-docs')
    

**Index Layout:** The indexer saves two files:

*   `state.json` - Full state including file path list (for incremental indexing)
*   `search.json` - Optimized state without file list (smaller, for search clients)

Search clients should load `search.json`. Indexers need `state.json` for incremental updates.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/advanced/custom-indexer#data-source-examples)

Data Source Examples
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   TypeScript
    
*   Python
    

**REST API:**

Copy

Ask AI

    async fetchAll(): Promise<FileEntry[]> {
      const response = await fetch("https://api.example.com/docs");
      const docs = await response.json();
      return docs.map((doc: any) => ({ path: doc.path, contents: doc.content }));
    }
    

**Database:**

Copy

Ask AI

    async fetchAll(): Promise<FileEntry[]> {
      const docs = await db.query("SELECT path, content FROM documents");
      return docs.map(doc => ({ path: doc.path, contents: doc.content }));
    }
    

**REST API:**

Copy

Ask AI

    def fetch_files(self):
        response = requests.get('https://api.example.com/docs')
        return [File(path=doc['path'], contents=doc['content']) for doc in response.json()]
    

**Database:**

Copy

Ask AI

    def fetch_files(self):
        docs = db.query('SELECT path, content FROM documents')
        return [File(path=doc.path, contents=doc.content) for doc in docs]

Automation
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Cron (Node.js):**

Copy

Ask AI

    0 * * * * cd /path/to/project && npx tsx indexer.ts
    

**Cron (Python):**

Copy

Ask AI

    0 * * * * cd /path/to/project && python indexer.py
    

**GitHub Actions:** See [GitHub Actions Auto-Indexing](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing)

# Local MCP Server - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#content-area)

Local MCP Server

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#prerequisites)
    
*   [Steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#steps)

*   [Also Works With](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#also-works-with)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Claude Desktop installed
*   An indexed project (see [Index and Search Code](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos)
    )
*   Augment API credentials

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#steps)

Steps
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#1-open-claude-desktop-config)

1\. Open Claude Desktop config

*   macOS
    
*   Windows
    

Copy

Ask AI

    open ~/Library/Application\ Support/Claude/claude_desktop_config.json
    

Copy

Ask AI

    %APPDATA%\Claude\claude_desktop_config.json
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#2-add-mcp-server-config)

2\. Add MCP server config

*   Local Filesystem
    
*   GitHub
    
*   GitLab
    
*   BitBucket
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "my-project": {
          "command": "npx",
          "args": ["ctxc", "mcp", "stdio", "-i", "my-project"],
          "env": {
            "AUGMENT_API_TOKEN": "your-token",
            "AUGMENT_API_URL": "https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/"
          }
        }
      }
    }
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "my-project": {
          "command": "npx",
          "args": ["ctxc", "mcp", "stdio", "-i", "my-project"],
          "env": {
            "AUGMENT_API_TOKEN": "your-token",
            "AUGMENT_API_URL": "https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/",
            "GITHUB_TOKEN": "ghp_..."
          }
        }
      }
    }
    

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "my-project": {
          "command": "npx",
          "args": ["ctxc", "mcp", "stdio", "-i", "my-project"],

            "AUGMENT_API_URL": "https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/",

      }

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#3-restart-claude-desktop)

3\. Restart Claude Desktop

Quit and reopen Claude Desktop.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#4-test-it)

4\. Test it

Ask Claude:

> Search for authentication logic in my-project

You should see Claude use the search tool and return code snippets.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#done)

Done!
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your agent can now search your codebase via the local MCP server.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#works-with-other-agents)

Works With Other Agents
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This same configuration works with any MCP-compatible agent:

*   **Claude Desktop** - Follow the steps above
*   **Claude Code** (VS Code extension) - Add to Claude Code’s MCP settings
*   **Cursor** - Configure in Cursor’s MCP settings
*   **GitHub Copilot** - Add to Copilot’s MCP configuration
*   **Custom agents** - Any tool that supports MCP stdio protocol

Each agent has its own config file location, but the MCP server configuration is the same.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration#also-works-with)

Also Works With
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Instead of… | Try… |
| --- | --- |
| One repo | Add multiple entries to `mcpServers` for different projects |
| Local index | S3-stored indexes with `--store s3` and `CC_S3_BUCKET` env var |
| Search only | Add `--search-only` to disable file reading |

[Index Website](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website)
[Remote MCP Server](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server)

⌘I

# Remote MCP Server - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Quickstart Recipes

Remote MCP Server

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#prerequisites)
    
*   [Steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#steps)
    
*   [1\. Install](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#1-install)
    
*   [2\. Set credentials](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#2-set-credentials)
    
*   [3\. Start the server](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#3-start-the-server)

*   [Also Works With](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#also-works-with)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

**For local MCP integration** with Claude Desktop, Claude Code, Cursor, or other agents, see [Local MCP Server](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration)
.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Node.js 18+
*   Augment API credentials
*   An indexed project (see [Index and Search Code](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos)
    )

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#steps)

Steps
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#1-install)

1\. Install

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @augmentcode/context-connectors @modelcontextprotocol/sdk
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#2-set-credentials)

2\. Set credentials

Copy

Ask AI

    export AUGMENT_API_TOKEN='your-token'
    export AUGMENT_API_URL='https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/'
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#3-start-the-server)

3\. Start the server

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc mcp http -i my-project --port 8080 --api-key "secret"
    

You should see:

Copy

Ask AI

    MCP HTTP server running at http://localhost:8080/mcp
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#4-test-with-curl)

4\. Test with curl

First, initialize a session:

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST http://localhost:8080/mcp \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -H "Accept: application/json, text/event-stream" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer secret" \
      -d '{
        "jsonrpc": "2.0",
        "id": 1,
        "method": "initialize",
        "params": {
          "protocolVersion": "2024-11-05",
          "capabilities": {},
          "clientInfo": { "name": "curl-test", "version": "1.0.0" }
        }
      }' -i
    

Note the `mcp-session-id` header in the response. Use it for subsequent requests:

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST http://localhost:8080/mcp \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -H "Accept: application/json, text/event-stream" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer secret" \
      -H "mcp-session-id: <session-id-from-initialize>" \
      -d '{
        "jsonrpc": "2.0",
        "id": 2,
        "method": "tools/call",
        "params": {
          "name": "search",
          "arguments": { "query": "authentication" }
        }
      }'
    

You should see JSON search results.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#done)

Done!
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your index is accessible via MCP over HTTP at `http://localhost:8080/mcp`. Remote clients can now search your codebase using the Model Context Protocol over HTTP.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server#also-works-with)

Also Works With
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Instead of… | Try… |
| --- | --- |
| localhost only | `--host 0.0.0.0` to accept external connections |
| No CORS | `--cors "*"` or `--cors "https://myapp.com"` for browser clients |
| Full access | `--search-only` to disable file operations |
| Local storage | `--store s3` with `CC_S3_BUCKET` for shared indexes |

[Local MCP Server](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration)
[Store Indexes in S3](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3)

⌘I

# Index and Search Code - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

On this page

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Node.js 18+
*   Augment API credentials (`AUGMENT_API_TOKEN`, `AUGMENT_API_URL`)
*   Git provider token with repo read access:
    *   GitHub: `GITHUB_TOKEN`
    *   GitLab: `GITLAB_TOKEN`
    *   BitBucket: `BITBUCKET_TOKEN`
*   For chat: An LLM API key (OpenAI, Anthropic, or Google)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#steps)

Steps
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#1-install)

1\. Install

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @augmentcode/context-connectors
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#2-set-credentials)

2\. Set credentials

*   GitHub
    
*   GitLab
    
*   BitBucket

Ask AI

    export AUGMENT_API_TOKEN='your-token'
    export AUGMENT_API_URL='https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/'
    export GITHUB_TOKEN='your-github-token'
    

Copy

Ask AI

    export AUGMENT_API_TOKEN='your-token'
    export AUGMENT_API_URL='https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/'
    export GITLAB_TOKEN='your-gitlab-token'
    

Copy

Ask AI

    export AUGMENT_API_TOKEN='your-token'
    export AUGMENT_API_URL='https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/'
    export BITBUCKET_TOKEN='your-bitbucket-token'
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#3-index-the-repository)

3\. Index the repository

*   GitHub
    
*   GitLab
    
*   Bitbucket
    

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc index github --owner facebook --repo react -i react
    

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc index gitlab --project mygroup/myrepo -i myrepo
    

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc index bitbucket --workspace myws --repo myrepo -i myrepo
    

You should see:

Copy

Ask AI

    Fetching file tree from facebook/react...
    Indexing complete: 2847 files indexed, 156 skipped
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#4-search)

4\. Search

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc search "How does the reconciliation algorithm work?" -i react
    

You should see an LLM-generated answer based on the codebase:

Copy

Ask AI

    Answer:
    
    Based on the code in packages/react-reconciler/src/ReactFiberReconciler.js...
    

For raw search results without LLM processing, add `--raw`:

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc search "reconciliation" -i react --raw
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#5-chat-optional)

5\. Chat (Optional)

For an interactive AI agent that can search and read the codebase:

Copy

Ask AI

    export OPENAI_API_KEY='your-openai-key'
    npx ctxc agent -i react --provider openai
    

You should see:

Copy

Ask AI

    Agent ready. Type your question or 'exit' to quit.
    
    >
    

Ask questions interactively:

Copy

Ask AI

    > How does React handle component updates?
    
    Searching: "component updates"...
    Reading: packages/react-reconciler/src/ReactFiberWorkLoop.js...
    
    Based on the code, React handles component updates by...
    

Type `exit` to quit.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#done)

Done!
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can now:

*   **Search** your codebase semantically with the `search` command
*   **Chat** with an AI agent that understands your code using the `agent` command

No need to clone the repository locally - Context Connectors fetches files directly from the Git provider API.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos#also-works-with)

Also Works With
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Instead of… | Try… |
| --- | --- |
| Default branch | `--ref main`, `--ref v1.0.0`, or `--ref abc123` for specific branch/tag/commit |
| Local storage | `--store s3` with `CC_S3_BUCKET` for team sharing |
| Manual updates | Set up [GitHub Actions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing)<br> to re-index on every push |
| Interactive chat | `npx ctxc agent -i react --provider openai "your question" --print` for single-question mode |
| OpenAI | `--provider anthropic` or `--provider google` for other LLM providers |
| Code repos | [Index websites](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website)<br> to chat with documentation sites |

[Overview](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/overview)
[Index Website](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website)

⌘I

Intent by Augment

Introducing Intent by Augment

On this page

**Public Beta** - Intent is in public beta. Some features may change as we continue to improve the experience.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#about-intent)

About Intent
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Intent is both a **spec-driven development app** and an **agent orchestration app**. These are two exciting paradigms that work together: specs keep your project aligned while multiple specialized agents execute work in parallel. The result is a new way to build software where you focus on intent and agents handle implementation.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#what-is-spec-driven-development)

What is spec-driven development?
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Spec-Driven Development puts the spec at the center of your workflow. Instead of writing code and hoping it matches the plan, you write the spec and let agents implement it. As they work, the spec updates to reflect what was actually built. Specs that are always accurate, agents that stay aligned, and code that matches intent.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#how-are-intent%E2%80%99s-specs-different)

How are Intent’s specs different?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When an agent completes work, the spec updates to reflect reality. When requirements change, updates propagate to all active agents. No more “what did we decide?” No more outdated PRDs. The spec is the source of truth because it maintains itself.

* * *

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#key-concepts)

Key concepts
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#spaces)

Spaces

When you create a prompt in Intent, it automatically creates a **Space** with its own dedicated git branch and worktree. This isolated environment allows agents to work on your code without affecting your main branch. ![Intent prompt to create a space](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/yZ9spAzQOYqM4m5R/images/intent_prompt_to_create_space.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=yZ9spAzQOYqM4m5R&q=85&s=59419abcec3a53d66b2acaea10ddd44e)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#coordinator-of-specialized-agents)

Coordinator of specialized agents

Intent’s multi-agent model mirrors how teams actually work. The **Coordination Agent** breaks down your spec into tasks. Specialist agents execute in parallel, each in their own context. The Coordinator keeps everything aligned and handles handoffs. When you submit a prompt, the Coordinator:

1.  **Analyzes your codebase** to understand the context and requirements
2.  **Drafts a Spec** that serves as a living document for the project
3.  **Generates tasks** for specialized agents to execute

You can stop the Coordinator at any time to manually edit the Spec, giving you full control over the direction of the work.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#the-spec-your-project%E2%80%99s-source-of-truth)

The spec: your project’s source of truth

The **Spec** is a self-maintaining document that serves as a running summary of:

*   The project goals and requirements
*   Tasks that need to be completed
*   Work that has been done
*   Assumptions, tradeoffs, and decisions

As the code changes, the Spec stays aligned and updated, ensuring developers and agents always work from the same context.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#parallel-work)

Parallel work

The Coordinator organizes work into coordinated efforts, assigning specialized agents to tackle specific tasks. Multiple agents can work in parallel on different aspects of the project, all staying synchronized through the shared spec. Run as many agents as the task needs. Intent keeps them in sync.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#review-stage-and-merge)

Review, stage, and merge

When agents complete their tasks, Intent notifies you. Navigate to the **Changes tab** to inspect all diffs and modifications made by the agents. From the Changes tab, you can:

*   **Inspect diffs** - Review all code changes side-by-side
*   **Create a PR** - Generate a pull request directly from the interface
*   **Auto-fill PR description** - Let the agent automatically generate a comprehensive PR description based on the work completed
*   **Stage changes** - Select which changes to include
*   **Merge** - Integrate the completed work back into your main branch

This workflow gives you full visibility and control over agent generated code changes, completing the cycle from intent to PR. ![Intent Changes tab](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/yZ9spAzQOYqM4m5R/images/intent_changes_to_pr.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=yZ9spAzQOYqM4m5R&q=85&s=0e1237f1bdd605bd8283ae01ce55e6fc)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#specialist-agents)

Specialist agents

Intent includes **6 specialist agent personas**, each designed for specific types of work. You can also create custom specialists in **Settings** to tailor agents to your specific workflow:

Investigate
-----------

Explore codebase, assess feasibility

Implement
---------

Execute implementation plans

Verify
------

Check implementations match specs

Critique
--------

Review specs for feasibility

Debug
-----

Analyze and fix issues

Code Review
-----------

Automated reviews with severity

The Coordinator assigns the right specialist for each task, ensuring expert-level execution across all aspects of your project.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#all-agents-are-powered-by-the-context-engine)

All agents are powered by the Context Engine

A multi-agent world needs even better context. Every agent in Intent is powered by Augment’s industry-leading [Context Engine](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview)
. Whether it’s the Coordinator planning your work or specialists executing tasks, they all share deep understanding of your entire codebase. Learn more about the [Context Engine](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/overview)
.

* * *

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#quickstart)

Quickstart
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#)

Download and Install Intent

Download the MacOS app from [augmentcode.com](https://augmentcode.com/)
. Windows coming soon. Install the application and launch Intent by Augment.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#)

Install Auggie CLI (Required for AI Features)

Install the Auggie CLI (`auggie`) from [augmentcode.com](https://augmentcode.com/)
. The Auggie CLI enables Intent to communicate with Augment’s AI agents and is required for full AI agent integration.

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#)

Create Your First Space

Describe your project in the prompt box and click **Create space** under the prompt box. Choose a name and location for your space, optionally link a Git repository, and add a description and tags for organization.

4

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#)

Your first session with the Coordinator

Your space opens with the Explorer to the left, Coordinator in the center, and the intial draft of the Spec to the right.

![Intent Coordinator and Spec panels](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/yZ9spAzQOYqM4m5R/images/intent_coordinator_spec_panels.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=yZ9spAzQOYqM4m5R&q=85&s=c0796b82081e4b5730a60fe7c4a50130)

* * *

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#key-features)

Key features
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#space-management)

Space management

Organize your development projects efficiently:

*   **Multiple Spaces**: Create separate spaces for different projects
*   **Rich Metadata**: Add descriptions, tags, and custom properties
*   **Git Integration**: View diffs, track changes, and manage repositories
*   **Activity Logging**: Comprehensive tracking of all space activities
*   **File Organization**: Track and manage project files with change detection

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#code-editor)

Code editor

Built-in code editing with professional features:

*   **Syntax Highlighting**: Support for 20+ programming languages
*   **CodeMirror Powered**: Industry-standard editor component
*   **Diff Viewer**: Side-by-side comparison of file changes
*   **Git Integration**: View and manage code changes inline

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#in-app-browser)

In-app browser

Stop switching between your IDE, terminal, browser, and git client. Intent has a **built-in Chrome browser** for previewing local changes. Preview your app without leaving the space.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#agent-integration)

Agent integration

Not every task needs the same model. Intent supports all major state-of-the-art models — mix and match based on what each task needs:

*   **Opus 4.5** — Complex architecture and planning
*   **Sonnet 4.5** — Rapid iteration
*   **GPT 5.2** — Deep code analysis and code review
*   **Haiku** — Fast, lightweight tasks

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#mcp-support)

MCP support

Full [Model Context Protocol](https://modelcontextprotocol.io/)
 (MCP) support. Connect external tools and data sources to extend what your agents can do — access databases, documentation, APIs, and more without leaving Intent.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#resumable-sessions)

Resumable sessions

Pick up exactly where you left off. Your space state persists across sessions — close Intent, reopen it tomorrow, and everything is exactly as you left it.

*   **Auto-commit** — Work is captured automatically as agents complete tasks
*   **Branch Management** — Branch creation, switching, and management built-in
*   **Persistent State** — Your progress is always saved

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/intent/overview#notes)

Notes

Keep your project documentation organized:

*   **Markdown Support**: Rich text editing with TipTap editor
*   **Tags & Organization**: Categorize notes with custom tags
*   **Full-Text Search**: Quickly find notes across all spaces
*   **Comments**: Add threaded comments to notes for collaboration

[CLI reference](https://docs.augmentcode.com/cli/reference)
[Install plugin](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/install-vim-neovim)

⌘I

# Available Models - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Models & Pricing

Available Models

On this page

*   [Current models](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#current-models)
    
*   [Choosing a model](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#choosing-a-model)
    
*   [Model pricing](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#model-pricing)
    
*   [Feature compatibility](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#feature-compatibility)
    
*   [Notes and transparency](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#notes-and-transparency)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#current-models)

Current models
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment uses world-class large language models together with our Context Engine. We currently support the following models:

*   Claude Haiku 4.5 by Anthropic
*   Claude Opus 4.5 by Anthropic
*   Claude Sonnet 4 by Anthropic
*   Claude Sonnet 4.5 by Anthropic
*   GPT-5.1 by OpenAI
*   GPT-5.2 by OpenAI

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#choosing-a-model)

Choosing a model
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can select the model directly using the Model Picker in the Augment.

*   In VS Code and JetBrains, open the Augment panel and use the model dropdown near the input box to switch models.
*   In Auggie CLI, use the `/model` slash command or pass the `--model` flag with the desired model.
*   Your selection applies only to Agent in that workspace and can be changed at any time.

If you don’t pick a model, Augment will use your last selection or the default set by your organization.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#model-pricing)

Model pricing
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment uses a credit-based pricing system. Different models consume credits at different rates based on their capabilities and costs:

*   **Sonnet 4.5**: Baseline credit consumption for balanced, complex tasks
*   **Haiku 4.5**: ~30% of Sonnet’s cost - ideal for quick, simple tasks
*   **GPT-5.1**: ~75% of Sonnet’s cost - great for medium-complexity work

**Premium models:**

*   **Opus 4.5**: ~167% of Sonnet’s cost - most capable model for the hardest tasks
*   **GPT-5.2**: ~133% of Sonnet’s cost - enhanced reasoning for complex tasks

Premium models require a credit-based usage plan and may consume credits at a higher rate than other models.

[Credit-Based Pricing\
--------------------\
\
Learn more about credit costs, see detailed examples, and discover tips for optimizing your credit usage](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#feature-compatibility)

Feature compatibility
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Both models support the core Augment Agent features:

*   Deep code understanding with Augment’s Context Engine
*   Tool use (integrations and MCP), file edits, and multi-step planning

Some behaviors (e.g., wording or style) may vary slightly between models. We’ll continue to refine prompts and guardrails to provide a consistent developer experience.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models#notes-and-transparency)

Notes and transparency
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   We may roll out model updates gradually. If you’re part of a staged rollout, different workspaces or teammates may see updates at different times.
*   For troubleshooting, you can share the request ID with our support team; they can confirm which model handled a specific request.

If you have questions about model availability or want to participate in early access programs, please reach out via Support.

[Quickstart](https://docs.augmentcode.com/quickstart)
[Credit-Based Pricing](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing)

⌘I

# Feedback - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Troubleshooting

Feedback

On this page

*   [Reporting a bug](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#reporting-a-bug)
    
*   [Feedback on completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#feedback-on-completions)
    
*   [Feedback on chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#feedback-on-chat)
    

Feedback helps us improve, and we encourage you to share your feedback on every aspect of using Augment—from suggestion and chat response quality, to user experience nusances, and even how we can improve getting your feedback.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#reporting-a-bug)

Reporting a bug

To report a bug, please [contact support](https://support.augmentcode.com/)
. Include as much detail to reproduce the problem as possible; screenshots and videos are very helpful.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#feedback-on-completions)

Feedback on completions

We are always balancing the needs for speed and accuracy. We want to know when you get a poor suggestion, hallucination, or a completion that actually doesn’t work. The History panel has a log of all of your completions; we encourage you to use it to send us feedback on the completions you’ve received.

Providing feedback directly in your IDE through the History panel is currently only available in Visual Studio Code.

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#)

Open the History panel

Open the History panel by pressing Cmd/Ctrl Shift P and then searching for `Augment: Show History` in the command menu.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#)

Find the completion you want to report

Recent completions are listed in reverse chronological order. Locate the completion you want to report and add complete the feedback form.

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#)

Submit your feedback

After completing the form, click either the red button for bad completions or the green button for good completions.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback#feedback-on-chat)

Feedback on chat

After each Chat interaction, you have the opportunity to provide feedback on the quality of the response. At the bottom of the response click either the thumbs up or thumbs down icon. Add additional information in the feedback field, and click `Send Feedback`.

[Using Teams](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide)
[Request IDs](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/request-id)

⌘I

# Install Augment GitHub App - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-github-app#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Configuration

Install Augment GitHub App

On this page

*   [Installation](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-github-app#installation)
    
*   [Permissions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-github-app#permissions)
    

The Augment GitHub App provides repository access for:

*   **Augment Code Review** — automated PR reviews
*   **Remote MCP Server** — cross-repo context for AI tools
*   **Augment for Slack** — codebase-aware Slack bot

All three features share the same GitHub App installation. If you’ve already installed the app for one feature (e.g., Code Review), you don’t need to install it again for the others.

The Augment GitHub App is only compatible with GitHub Enterprise Cloud and github.com. GitHub Enterprise Server is not currently supported.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-github-app#installation)

Installation
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Install the Augment GitHub App from the Customer UI to link your Augment account to the GitHub App:

1.  Visit one of the following configuration pages:
    *   [Code Review Settings](https://app.augmentcode.com/settings/code-review)
         — for Code Review setup
    *   [MCP Configuration](https://app.augmentcode.com/settings/mcp)
         — for Remote MCP Server setup
2.  Click on the **Install GitHub App** button to begin the installation process.
3.  Grant access to your desired repositories.

Organization owners and repository admins can install the app directly; others will need owner approval. See [GitHub documentation](https://docs.github.com/en/apps/using-github-apps/installing-a-github-app-from-a-third-party)
 for details. ![Installing the GitHub app on a single repository](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/install-github-app.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=333c129e393ab4b32f04c3940492cf1c) You can modify repository access anytime in the Augment GitHub App settings.

Who can install the Augment GitHub App?

To install the Augment GitHub App, you will need to be an Administrator of your GitHub organization. To find who the Administrators are, visit your GitHub organization settings page and click on “People.” Administrators are listed under “Owners.”![GitHub Admins](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/V_zyvyrMw4E2FxEk/images/code-review-owners.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=V_zyvyrMw4E2FxEk&q=85&s=1f74e1e9fb88262a6a1399af1db2e06c)

If your firewall configuration, allowlist or network policy requires a static IP for this integration, please refer to our [static IP address](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/static-ip-support#allow-augment-traffic-from-static-ips)
 documentation.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-github-app#permissions)

Permissions
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Augment GitHub App requests the following permissions:

*   Contents, read-only: Clone repositories
*   Pull Requests, read and write: Read pull requests and post comments to pull requests
*   Issues, read-only: Read top-level PRs / Issues
*   Organization Members, read-only: Read members of an organization, to distinguish internal and external users and their access levels to Augment features

[Rules & Guidelines](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/guidelines)
[Network configuration](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration)

⌘I

---

# Store Indexes in S3 - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Quickstart Recipes

Store Indexes in S3

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#prerequisites)
    
*   [Steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#steps)
    
*   [1\. Install](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#1-install)
    
*   [2\. Set credentials](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#2-set-credentials)
    
*   [3\. Index to S3](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#3-index-to-s3)
    
*   [4\. Search from S3](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#4-search-from-s3)
    
*   [Done!](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#done)
    
*   [Also Works With](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#also-works-with)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

S3 storage enables two key use cases:

*   **Team Sharing**: Multiple team members can search the same index
*   **Application Data**: Build apps that manage per-user indexes in S3

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Node.js 18+
*   Augment API credentials
*   AWS credentials with S3 read/write access
*   An S3 bucket

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#steps)

Steps
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#1-install)

1\. Install

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @augmentcode/context-connectors @aws-sdk/client-s3
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#2-set-credentials)

2\. Set credentials

Copy

Ask AI

    export AUGMENT_API_TOKEN='your-token'
    export AUGMENT_API_URL='https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/'
    export AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID='your-key'
    export AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY='your-secret'
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#3-index-to-s3)

3\. Index to S3

Copy

Ask AI

    export CC_S3_BUCKET='my-team-bucket'
    npx ctxc index github --owner myorg --repo myrepo -i my-project \
      --store s3
    

You should see:

Copy

Ask AI

    Fetching file tree from myorg/myrepo...
    Indexing complete: 142 files indexed, 0 skipped
    Stored to s3://my-team-bucket/context-connectors/my-project/
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#4-search-from-s3)

4\. Search from S3

Anyone with AWS credentials can now search:

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc search "How does authentication work?" \
      -i s3://my-team-bucket/context-connectors/my-project
    

Indexes are stored under a `context-connectors/` prefix in your bucket. Include this prefix when searching.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#done)

Done!
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your index is stored in S3 at `s3://my-team-bucket/context-connectors/my-project/`. Share the S3 URL with your team.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3#also-works-with)

Also Works With
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Instead of… | Try… |
| --- | --- |
| AWS S3 | MinIO: set `CC_S3_ENDPOINT` and `CC_S3_FORCE_PATH_STYLE=true` |
| AWS S3 | DigitalOcean Spaces, Backblaze B2, Cloudflare R2 (use `CC_S3_ENDPOINT`) |
| Manual indexing | [Auto-index on push](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook)<br> with GitHub webhooks |

[Remote MCP Server](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/remote-mcp-server)
[GitHub Actions Auto-Indexing](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing)

⌘I

# Credit-Based Pricing - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Models & Pricing

Credit-Based Pricing

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#overview)
    
*   [Credit costs by model](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#credit-costs-by-model)
    
*   [Example tasks](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#example-tasks)
    
*   [Sonnet task: Fix a 500 error in an API endpoint](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#sonnet-task-fix-a-500-error-in-an-api-endpoint)
    
*   [Opus task: Design and implement a multi-tenant billing system](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#opus-task-design-and-implement-a-multi-tenant-billing-system)
