*   [Related resources](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#related-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#overview)

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment uses a credit-based pricing system where different models consume credits at different rates to reflect their power and cost. This gives you the flexibility to choose the right model for each task based on complexity and budget.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#credit-costs-by-model)

Credit costs by model
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each model consumes credits at different rates based on its capabilities and underlying costs. Here’s how the models compare:

| Model | Credits per task\* | Relative cost | Best for |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Claude Sonnet 4.5** | 293 credits | Baseline (100%) | Balanced capability. Ideal for medium or large tasks and is optimized for complex or multi-step work. |
| **Claude Opus 4.5** | 488 credits | 167% of Sonnet | Most capable model. Best for the hardest tasks requiring deep reasoning, nuanced understanding, and exceptional quality. |
| **Claude Haiku 4.5** | 88 credits | 30% of Sonnet | Lightweight, fast reasoning. Best for quick edits and small tasks. |
| **GPT-5.1** | 219 credits | 75% of Sonnet | Advanced reasoning and context. Builds great plans and works well for medium-size tasks. |
| **GPT-5.2** | 390 credits | 133% of Sonnet | Enhanced reasoning capabilities. Excellent for complex tasks requiring long chains of thought. |

\*Based on a standard medium-complexity task. Actual credit consumption varies based on task complexity, context size, and response length.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#example-tasks)

Example tasks
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To illustrate the credit differences, here are examples of tasks and how much they cost with each model.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#sonnet-task-fix-a-500-error-in-an-api-endpoint)

Sonnet task: Fix a 500 error in an API endpoint

> The `/api/users/:id` endpoint returns 500 errors when a user has no associated organization. Add null checking and return a 404 with a clear error message instead. Test that users with organizations still work correctly.

**Credit cost:** 293 credits with Sonnet 4.5

| Model | Credits | Savings |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Sonnet 4.5** | 293 credits | —   |
| **Opus 4.5** | 488 credits | Use for harder tasks |
| **GPT-5.2** | 390 credits | Use for harder tasks |
| **Haiku 4.5** | 88 credits | 205 credits saved |
| **GPT-5.1** | 219 credits | 74 credits saved |

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#opus-task-design-and-implement-a-multi-tenant-billing-system)

Opus task: Design and implement a multi-tenant billing system

> Our B2B SaaS platform needs a multi-tenant billing system. Currently we have a simple Stripe integration for single subscriptions, but we need to support:
> 
> 1.  **Usage-based billing**: Track API calls per tenant with tiered pricing (first 10k calls free, then $0.001/call)
> 2.  **Seat-based licensing**: Charge per active user with volume discounts
> 3.  **Hybrid plans**: Combine base subscription + usage overages
> 4.  **Invoice generation**: Monthly invoices with line-item breakdown by workspace
> 5.  **Billing isolation**: Each tenant’s billing data must be completely isolated
> 
> Design the database schema, implement the metering service, integrate with Stripe’s usage-based billing API, and ensure we handle edge cases like mid-cycle plan changes, prorations, and failed payments. Consider how this will scale to 10k+ tenants.

**Credit cost:** 976 credits with Opus 4.5

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#monitoring-credit-usage)

Monitoring credit usage
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can track your credit consumption in multiple places:

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#in-your-ide)

In your IDE

*   **VS Code**: View credit usage in the Augment panel
*   **JetBrains**: Check the Augment tool window for usage stats
*   **Auggie CLI**: Monitor credits used per session

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#on-the-web)

On the web

Visit [app.augmentcode.com](https://app.augmentcode.com/)
 to access detailed dashboards that show:

*   Total credits used by your team
*   Credit usage per team member
*   Breakdown by model and activity
*   Usage trends over time
*   Remaining credits in your plan

Team administrators can access more detailed analytics to help optimize team usage and identify opportunities to save credits by using more efficient models for appropriate tasks.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#understanding-your-usage-breakdown)

Understanding your usage breakdown
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you view your usage analytics, you’ll see credits organized by both **model** and **activity type**. Here’s what each activity type means:

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#session-types)

Session types

These are the main session types you can use with Augment:

| Activity | What it is |
| --- | --- |
| **Chat** | Conversational chat session |
| **Agent** | Local agent session (in your IDE) |
| **RemoteAgent** | Cloud-based agent session (asynchronous) |
| **CliAgent** | Command-line agent session (Auggie CLI) |

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#optional-features)

Optional features

| Activity | What it is |
| --- | --- |
| **Prompt Enhancer** | Appears when you use the Prompt Enhancer feature to improve your prompts before sending them |
| **Code Review** | Automated code review for pull requests (when enabled for your repository) |

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#background-activities)

Background activities

Augment performs lightweight processing in the background to keep your experience smooth:

| Activity | What it does |
| --- | --- |
| **Context Compression** | Summarizes conversation history to keep long sessions fast and responsive |
| **System** | General background processing that helps Augment work smoothly |

These background activities use a small fraction of your total credit consumption. In most workflows, they’re a minor part of overall usage.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#tips-for-optimizing-credit-usage)

Tips for optimizing credit usage
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Match the model to the task**: Use Haiku for simple tasks, GPT-5.1 for medium tasks, Sonnet for complex work, and Opus for the hardest challenges
2.  **Be specific in your prompts**: Clear, detailed instructions help models work more efficiently
3.  **Break down large tasks**: Sometimes splitting a complex task into smaller ones can be more credit-efficient
4.  **Review usage patterns**: Check your dashboards regularly to identify optimization opportunities
5.  **Set team guidelines**: Establish best practices for model selection within your team

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#frequently-asked-questions)

Frequently asked questions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

How are credits calculated?

Credits are consumed based on the model used, the size of the context (code being analyzed), and the length of the response generated. More complex tasks that require analyzing more code or generating longer responses will consume more credits.

What happens if I run out of credits?

When you run out of credits, you’ll need to upgrade your plan or wait until your credits reset at the beginning of your next billing cycle. Team administrators can purchase additional credits or upgrade the team plan at any time.

Can I switch models mid-conversation?

Currently, you can switch models mid-conversation in **Auggie CLI** using the `/model` command. Each message will consume credits based on the model selected for that specific message. Model switching mid-conversation is not yet available in the IDE extensions (VS Code, JetBrains), but you can change your model selection between separate conversations.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/credit-based-pricing#related-resources)

# Index Website - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Quickstart Recipes

Index Website

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#prerequisites)
    
*   [Steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#steps)
    
*   [1\. Install](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#1-install)
    
*   [2\. Set credentials](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#2-set-credentials)
    
*   [3\. Index the site](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#3-index-the-site)
    
*   [4\. Search](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#4-search)
    
*   [5\. Chat (Optional)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#5-chat-optional)
    
*   [Done!](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#done)
    
*   [Limitations](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#limitations)
    
*   [Also Works With](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#also-works-with)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Node.js 18+
*   Augment API credentials
*   For chat: An LLM API key (OpenAI, Anthropic, or Google)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#steps)

Steps
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#1-install)

1\. Install

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @augmentcode/context-connectors
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#2-set-credentials)

2\. Set credentials

Copy

Ask AI

    export AUGMENT_API_TOKEN='your-token'
    export AUGMENT_API_URL='https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/'
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#3-index-the-site)

3\. Index the site

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc index website --url https://docs.example.com -i example-docs
    

You should see:

Copy

Ask AI

    Crawling https://docs.example.com...
    Indexing complete: 87 pages indexed, 12 skipped
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#4-search)

4\. Search

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc search "how to configure SSO" -i example-docs
    

You should see an LLM-generated answer based on the documentation:

Copy

Ask AI

    Answer:
    
    Based on the documentation at https://docs.example.com/auth/sso, SSO can be configured by...
    

For raw search results without LLM processing, add `--raw`:

Copy

Ask AI

    npx ctxc search "SSO" -i example-docs --raw
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#5-chat-optional)

5\. Chat (Optional)

For an interactive AI agent that can search and read the documentation:

Copy

Ask AI

    export OPENAI_API_KEY='your-openai-key'
    npx ctxc agent -i example-docs --provider openai
    

You should see:

Copy

Ask AI

    Agent ready. Type your question or 'exit' to quit.
    
    >
    

Ask questions interactively:

Copy

Ask AI

    > How do I set up SSO with Okta?
    
    Searching: "SSO Okta setup"...
    Reading: https://docs.example.com/auth/sso-okta...
    
    Based on the documentation, to set up SSO with Okta you need to...
    

Type `exit` to quit.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#done)

Done!
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can now:

*   **Search** the documentation semantically with the `search` command
*   **Chat** with an AI agent that understands the docs using the `agent` command

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#limitations)

Limitations
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Only static HTML is indexed. JavaScript-rendered content (SPAs) won’t work.
*   Only pages linked from the starting URL are discovered.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-website#also-works-with)

Also Works With
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Instead of… | Try… |
| --- | --- |
| Single site | Index multiple sites with different `-i` names |
| Local storage | `--store s3` with `CC_S3_BUCKET` for team sharing |
| Interactive chat | `npx ctxc agent -i example-docs --provider openai "your question" --print` for single-question mode |
| OpenAI | `--provider anthropic` or `--provider google` for other LLM providers |

[Index and Search Code](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/index-git-repos)
[Local MCP Server](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/claude-desktop-integration)

⌘I

*   [Changing Plans](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#changing-plans)
    
*   [Managing Seats](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#managing-seats)
    
*   [Troubleshooting](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#troubleshooting)
    
*   [Best Practices](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#best-practices)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#about-teams)

About Teams
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If multiple people from your organization use Augment Code through our [Indie, Standard or Max plan](https://augmentcode.com/pricing)
, Teams gathers accounts together for better collaboration. Teams simplify account management, offer better access control and centralize billing. Team administrators have special privileges to invite members, manage seats, change plans, and control team settings. Teams are not available for Enterprise plans since this plan by defaults groups the entire organization.

Team settings and billing management are only accessible to accounts assigned as the administrator. Individual team members can view team information but cannot modify settings or manage subscriptions. To change which account is set as the administrator, contact [Augment Code Support](https://portal.usepylon.com/augment-code/forms/augment-support)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#team-roles-and-permissions)

Team Roles and Permissions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#administrator-role)

Administrator Role

*   Can invite new team members or cancel pending invitations
*   Can remove team members
*   Can manage team seats (increase/decrease)
*   Can change team plans
*   Can view and manage billing information

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#member-role)

Member Role

*   Can view team information
*   Can leave the team (remove themselves)
*   Cannot invite or remove other members
*   Cannot manage billing or change plans

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#adding-team-members)

Adding Team Members
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add team members, you must be an administrator with available seats on your plan.

1.  **Navigate to Team from Account** - Go to your [Account](https://app.augmentcode.com/account/)
    , and then select the “Team” tab
2.  **Initiate Invitation** - Click “Add team member,” enter the email address, and click “Send invitation”
3.  **Invitation Status** - The invitation appears as “Pending” in your team members list and counts toward your seat allocation
4.  **Acceptance** - The invitee receives an email with instructions to join. Once they authenticate with their Augment account (or create one), they become an active team member

Invitations expire after 7 days. Pending invitations can be cancelled before acceptance. If your team is at capacity, add more seats before inviting new members. You can send multiple invitations simultaneously using comma-separated emails.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#removing-team-members)

Removing Team Members
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To remove team members, you must be an administrator. Members can also remove themselves from a team.

1.  **Navigate to Team from Account** - Go to your [Account](https://app.augmentcode.com/account/)
    , select the “Team” tab, and find the member you want to remove
2.  **Remove Member** - Click the three-dot menu (⋮) next to the member’s name, select “Remove Member,” and confirm the removal
3.  **After Removal** - The member immediately loses access to team resources and their account reverts to individual status. For paid plans, the seat becomes available at the next billing cycle.

Leaving? [Ask Augment Code Support](https://support.augmentcode.com/)
 to grant administrator access to another account before removing yourself if you’re the only administrator.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#cancelling-pending-invitations)

Cancelling Pending Invitations

To cancel a pending invitation, navigate to the team members list, filter by “Pending” status, click the three-dot menu next to the pending invitation, and select “Cancel Invitation.”

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#managing-team-plans-and-subscriptions)

Managing Team Plans and Subscriptions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment offers flexible plans to meet your team’s needs. Visit [augmentcode.com/pricing](https://augmentcode.com/pricing)
 for current plan options and pricing.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#changing-plans)

Changing Plans

To change your team’s plan, you must be a team administrator with a valid payment method for paid plans.

1.  **Access Plan Selection** - Go to [Account](https://app.augmentcode.com/account/)
     then select Subscription and click “Change Plan” or “Upgrade”
2.  **Select New Plan** - Review available plans, pricing, and included features for your team size
3.  **Configure Details** - Set the number of seats needed and review pricing calculations
4.  **Confirm** - Add or update your payment method if needed, review prorated charges or credits, and confirm the plan change

Plan changes may be immediate (upgrades, free to paid, trial to paid) or take effect at the end of your billing cycle (downgrades). Prorated charges and credits are calculated automatically for mid-cycle changes.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#managing-seats)

Managing Seats

**Adding Seats**

1.  **Navigate to Team Settings** - Go to [Account](https://app.augmentcode.com/account/)
     then the Team tab and click “Manage Seats”
2.  **Increase Seat Count** - Use the number control to increase seats and review the new monthly cost
3.  **Save Changes** - Click “Save changes” to confirm. Additional seats are billed immediately (prorated) and the new monthly rate takes effect immediately

**Removing Seats**

1.  **Check Current Usage** - Ensure you have unused seats. You cannot reduce seats below your active members plus pending invitations
2.  **Decrease Seat Count** - Navigate to “Manage Seats,” reduce the number using the control, and save changes
3.  **Billing Impact** - Removed seats remain active until the next billing cycle. Credits are applied at the next billing period

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Cannot add members - no seats available**

*   Purchase additional seats or remove inactive members
*   Cancel pending invitations to free up seat allocation

**Payment method required**

*   Add a valid credit card in Account > Billing
*   Ensure your payment method is not expired
*   Contact support for payment issues

**Cannot remove last admin**

*   Promote another member to admin first before removing yourself

**Invitation expired**

*   Resend the invitation from the Team tab
*   Verify the correct email address was used
*   Check spam folders for the invitation email

For additional help, contact [Support](https://portal.usepylon.com/augment-code/forms/augment-support)
 or visit [docs.augmentcode.com](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)
.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/teams/teams-admin-guide#best-practices)

Best Practices
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Regular Audits** - Review team membership monthly, remove inactive members promptly, and monitor seat utilization to optimize costs. **Invitation Management** - Verify email addresses before sending invitations and follow up with invitees directly. Cancel unaccepted invitations after 48 hours to free up seats. **Billing Optimization** - Right-size your seat count and plan seat changes for billing cycle boundaries to avoid prorated charges. **Security** - Remove members immediately upon departure, regularly review admin permissions, and use company email addresses for all team members.

[API reference](https://docs.augmentcode.com/analytics/api-reference)
[Feedback](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback)

⌘I

# GitHub Actions Auto-Indexing - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Quickstart Recipes

GitHub Actions Auto-Indexing

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#prerequisites)
    
*   [Steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#steps)
    
*   [1\. Create the workflow file](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#1-create-the-workflow-file)
    
*   [2\. Set up GitHub repository secrets](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#2-set-up-github-repository-secrets)
    
*   [3\. Commit and push](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#3-commit-and-push)
    
*   [4\. Verify it’s working](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#4-verify-it%E2%80%99s-working)
    
*   [Done!](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#done)
    
*   [Also Works With](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#also-works-with)
    
*   [How It Works](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#how-it-works)
    
*   [Advanced: Using S3 Storage](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#advanced-using-s3-storage)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Connectors is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   A GitHub repository
*   Augment API credentials

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#steps)

Steps
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#1-create-the-workflow-file)

1\. Create the workflow file

Create `.github/workflows/augment-index.yml` in your repository:

Copy

Ask AI

    name: Index Repository
    
    on:
      push:
        branches:
          - main
      workflow_dispatch:  # Allow manual triggering
    
    jobs:
      index:
        runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    
        steps:
          - name: Checkout repository
            uses: actions/checkout@v4
    
          - name: Setup Node.js
            uses: actions/setup-node@v4
            with:
              node-version: '20'
    
          - name: Restore index state
            uses: actions/cache@v4
            with:
              path: .augment-index-state
              key: augment-index-${{ github.ref_name }}-${{ github.sha }}
              restore-keys: |
                augment-index-${{ github.ref_name }}-
    
          - name: Index repository
            run: |
              npx @augmentcode/context-connectors index github \
                --owner ${{ github.repository_owner }} \
                --repo ${{ github.event.repository.name }} \
                --ref ${{ github.sha }} \
                -i ${{ github.repository_owner }}/${{ github.event.repository.name }}
            env:
              GITHUB_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
              AUGMENT_API_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.AUGMENT_API_TOKEN }}
              AUGMENT_API_URL: ${{ secrets.AUGMENT_API_URL }}
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#2-set-up-github-repository-secrets)

2\. Set up GitHub repository secrets

Go to your repository **Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions** and add:

| Secret Name | Value |
| --- | --- |
| `AUGMENT_API_TOKEN` | Your Augment API token |
| `AUGMENT_API_URL` | Your tenant URL (e.g., `https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/`) |

**How to get your credentials:**

Copy

Ask AI

    # Login to Augment
    auggie login
    
    # Print your credentials
    auggie token print
    

This outputs your `accessToken` (use for `AUGMENT_API_TOKEN`) and `tenantURL` (use for `AUGMENT_API_URL`).

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#3-commit-and-push)

3\. Commit and push

Copy

Ask AI

    git add .github/workflows/augment-index.yml
    git commit -m "Add Augment indexing workflow"
    git push
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#4-verify-it%E2%80%99s-working)

4\. Verify it’s working

Go to your repository’s **Actions** tab. You should see the “Index Repository” workflow running. Once complete, you can search your index:

Copy

Ask AI

    export AUGMENT_API_TOKEN='your-token'
    export AUGMENT_API_URL='https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com/'
    npx ctxc search "authentication logic" -i myorg/myrepo
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#done)

Done!
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your repository will now automatically re-index on every push to the main branch. The workflow uses GitHub Actions cache to store index state for efficient incremental updates.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#also-works-with)

Also Works With
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Instead of… | Try… |
| --- | --- |
| Main branch only | Edit the workflow to add more branches: `branches: [main, develop]` |
| GitHub cache | Use S3 storage: add `--store s3` and set `CC_S3_BUCKET` env var |
| Custom index name | Change the `-i` value to your preferred name |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#how-it-works)

How It Works
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The workflow:

1.  **Triggers** on every push to your main branch
2.  **Restores** the previous index state from GitHub Actions cache
3.  **Indexes** the repository using the GitHub API (no checkout needed for indexing)
4.  **Caches** the new index state for the next run

This approach is much faster than full re-indexing on every push.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/github-actions-indexing#advanced-using-s3-storage)

Advanced: Using S3 Storage
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For production use or team sharing, you can store indexes in S3 instead of GitHub cache:

1.  Edit `.github/workflows/augment-index.yml`
2.  Add S3 configuration to the command:

Copy

Ask AI

    - name: Index repository
      run: |
        npx @augmentcode/context-connectors index github \
          --owner ${{ github.repository_owner }} \
          --repo ${{ github.event.repository.name }} \
          --ref ${{ github.sha }} \
          -i ${{ github.repository_owner }}/${{ github.event.repository.name }} \
          --store s3
      env:
        GITHUB_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
        AUGMENT_API_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.AUGMENT_API_TOKEN }}
        AUGMENT_API_URL: ${{ secrets.AUGMENT_API_URL }}
        AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID: ${{ secrets.AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID }}
        AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY: ${{ secrets.AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY }}
        CC_S3_BUCKET: my-team-indexes
    

3.  Add AWS credentials to repository secrets

This allows multiple repositories or team members to share the same index.

[Store Indexes in S3](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/share-with-s3)
[Auto-Index with Webhooks](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/context-connectors/quickstart/auto-index-webhook)

⌘I

Finding a Request ID for Chat
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/request-id#)

Open the Chat panel

Open the Chat panel by clicking the Augment icon![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-chat.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=aa776a96f49e4d86cb0a0d7cef78cc67)in the action bar on the left side of your editor.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/request-id#)

Open the chat thread

If the chat reply you are interested is in a previous chat thread, find the chat thread by clicking the at the top of the chat panel and clicking the relevant chat thread.

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/request-id#)

Find the request ID

Find the reply in question and click the icon above the reply to copy the request ID to your clipboard.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/request-id#finding-a-request-id-for-completions)

Finding a Request ID for Completions
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/request-id#)

Open the History panel

Open the History panel by pressing Cmd/Ctrl Shift P and then searching for `Augment: Show History` in the command menu.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/request-id#)

Find the request ID

Recent requests are listed in reverse chronological order. Locate the request you are interested in and copy the request ID by clicking on the request ID, for example:  
`-- Request ID: 7f67c0dd-4c80-4167-9383-8013b18836cb`

# Jetbrains panel steals focus - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Troubleshooting

Jetbrains panel steals focus

On this page

*   [About focus issues in JetBrains IDEs](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus#about-focus-issues-in-jetbrains-ides)
    
*   [Enable off-screen rendering](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus#enable-off-screen-rendering)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus#about-focus-issues-in-jetbrains-ides)

About focus issues in JetBrains IDEs
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Some users on Linux systems have reported that the Augment Chat window steals focus from the editor while typing. This can interrupt your workflow and make it difficult to use the IDE effectively. This issue can be resolved by enabling off-screen rendering in your JetBrains IDE.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus#enable-off-screen-rendering)

Enable off-screen rendering

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus#)

Open the Custom Properties editor

From the menu bar, go to Help > Edit Custom Properties.... If the `idea.properties` file doesn’t exist yet, you’ll be prompted to create it.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus#)

Add the off-screen rendering property

Add the following line to the properties file:

Copy

Ask AI

    augment.off.screen.rendering=true
    

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus#)

Save and restart your IDE

Save the file and restart your JetBrains IDE for the changes to take effect.

After restarting, the Augment panel should no longer steal focus from the editor while you’re typing.

[Request IDs](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/request-id)
[Jetbrains UI issues](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues)

⌘I

# Jetbrains UI issues - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Troubleshooting

Jetbrains UI issues

On this page

*   [About UI issues in JetBrains IDEs](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues#about-ui-issues-in-jetbrains-ides)
    
*   [Disable out-of-process rendering](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues#disable-out-of-process-rendering)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues#about-ui-issues-in-jetbrains-ides)

About UI issues in JetBrains IDEs
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Some users on newer versions of JetBrains IDEs (2025.1 and above) have reported that the Augment panel is white, blank or not displaying anything at all. These issues stem from a change to the way JetBrains renders webviews, which is now done in an out-of-process manner. Disabling out-of-process rendering has resolved a number of problems for users. This is a known issue that impacts multiple plugins in the Jetbrains ecosystem. JetBrains is tracking the issue in IJPL-186252. **Note**: If you are using a **JetBrains IDE 2025.2.3 on Windows**, we do not recommend disabling out-of-process rendering due to a bug where the WebViews will render JS and CSS in plain text making it difficult to use Augment and any other WebViews. There is a workaround for this issue [described here](https://youtrack.jetbrains.com/issue/JBR-9462/Markdown-rendering-broken-with-ide.browser.jcef.out-of-process.enabledfalse-after-upgrading-to-PyCharm-2025.2.3#focus=Comments-27-12792022.0-0)
. If you experience issues after following the steps below, please [contact support](https://support.augmentcode.com/)
 for further assistance.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues#disable-out-of-process-rendering)

Disable out-of-process rendering

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues#)

Open the Custom Properties editor

From the menu bar, go to Help > Edit Custom Properties.... If the `idea.properties` file doesn’t exist yet, you’ll be prompted to create it.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues#)

Add the out-of-process rendering property

Add the following line to the properties file:

Copy

Ask AI

    ide.browser.jcef.out-of-process.enabled=false
    

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-rendering-issues#)

Save and restart your IDE

Save the file and restart your JetBrains IDE for the changes to take effect.

After restarting, the Augment panel should render more consistently.

[Jetbrains panel steals focus](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/jetbrains-stealing-focus)

⌘I

# Install Augment for Slack - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#content-area)

Slack

Install Augment for Slack

On this page

*   [About Augment for Slack](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#about-augment-for-slack)
    
*   [Installing Augment for Slack](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#installing-augment-for-slack)
    
*   [1\. Install GitHub App](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#1-install-github-app)
    
*   [2\. Install Slack App](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#2-install-slack-app)
    
*   [3\. Add Augment to the Slack Navigation Bar](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#3-add-augment-to-the-slack-navigation-bar)
    

The Augment GitHub App is compatible with GitHub.com and GitHub Enterprise Cloud. GitHub Enterprise Server is not currently supported.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#about-augment-for-slack)

About Augment for Slack
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment for Slack brings the power of Augment Chat to your team’s Slack workspace. Mention @Augment in any channel or start a DM with Augment to have deep codebase-aware conversations with your team. _To protect your confidential information, Augment will not include repository context in responses when used in shared channels with external members._

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#installing-augment-for-slack)

Installing Augment for Slack
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#1-install-github-app)

1\. Install GitHub App

[Install Augment GitHub App\
--------------------------\
\
Connect your GitHub repositories to Augment](https://github.com/apps/augmentcode/installations/new)

To enable Augment’s rich codebase-awareness, install the Augment GitHub App and grant access to your desired repositories. We recommend authorizing only the repositories you want accessible to Augment Slack users. ![Installing the GitHub app on a single repository](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/install-github-app.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=333c129e393ab4b32f04c3940492cf1c) For details on permissions, troubleshooting, and who can install the app, see [Install Augment GitHub App](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-github-app)
.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#2-install-slack-app)

2\. Install Slack App

[Install Augment for Slack\
-------------------------\
\
Slack App for Augment Code](https://slack.com/oauth/v2/authorize?client_id=3751018318864.7878669571030&scope=app_mentions:read,channels:history,channels:read,chat:write,groups:history,groups:read,im:history,im:read,im:write,mpim:history,mpim:read,mpim:write,reactions:read,reactions:write,users.profile:read,users:read,users:read.email,groups:write,commands,assistant:write&user_scope=identity.basic)

Once you have the GitHub App installed, install the Augment Slack App. You’ll need an Augment account and correct permissions to install Slack apps for your workspace. Any workspace member can use the Slack app once installed. Contact us if you need to restrict access to specific channels or users.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-slack-app#3-add-augment-to-the-slack-navigation-bar)

3\. Add Augment to the Slack Navigation Bar

Make Augment easily accessible by adding it to Slack’s assistant-view navigation bar:

1.  Click your profile picture → **Preferences** → **Navigation**
2.  Under **App agents & assistants**, select **Augment**

_Note: Each user can customize this setting in their preferences._

### Next steps

[Using Augment for Slack](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/slack)

[Troubleshooting](https://docs.augmentcode.com/codereview/troubleshooting)
[Using Augment in Slack](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/slack)

# Instructions - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/instructions#content-area)

Visual Studio Code

Instructions

On this page

*   [About Instructions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/instructions#about-instructions)

Availability

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/instructions#about-instructions)

About Instructions
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment’s Instructions let you use natural language prompts to insert new code or modify your existing code. Instructions can be initiated by hitting Cmd/Ctrl I and entering an instruction inside the input box that appears in the diff view. The change will be applied as a diff to be reviewed before accepting.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/instructions#using-instructions)

Using Instructions
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start a new Instruction, there are two options. You can select & highlight the code you want to change or place your cursor where you want new code to be added, then press Cmd/Ctrl I. You’ll be taken to a diff view where you can enter your prompt and see the results. For example, you can generate new functions based on existing code:

Copy

Ask AI

    > Add a getUser function that takes userId as a parameter
    

![Augment Instructions Diff](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/instructions.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=30ae9550ad8b82d4b84ee39aeeee2e76) Your change will be made as a diff, so you can review the suggested updates before modifying your code. Use the following shortcuts or click the options in the UI to accept or reject the changes.

*   MacOS
    
*   Windows/Linux
    

| Action | Shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Start instruction | Cmd I |
| Accept | Return |
| Reject | Esc |

| Action | Shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Start instruction | Ctrl I |
| Accept | Return |
| Reject | Esc |

[Next Edit](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/next-edit)
[Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions)

# Context Engine MCP - Augment

Context Engine MCP

Context Engine MCP

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#what-is-the-context-engine)

What is the Context Engine?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every AI uses the same models. **Context is the difference.** Augment’s Context Engine maintains a live understanding of your entire stack:

*   **Semantic understanding** — Not just grep. A full search engine for code that understands meaning, not just text.
*   **Relationship awareness** — Understands how files connect across repos, services, and architectures.
*   **More than code** — Indexes commit history, codebase patterns, external sources (docs, tickets), and tribal knowledge.
*   **Smart curation** — Retrieves only what matters and compresses context without losing information.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#local-vs-remote-server)

Local vs Remote Server
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Aspect | Local Server | Remote Server |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Best for** | Making edits, new features, active development | Adding to codebase, understanding/talking to code |
| **What’s indexed** | Working directory in real-time | Selected repos’ default branches (chosen during GitHub App install) |
| **Setup** | Run Auggie CLI locally | GitHub App + [app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration](https://app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration) |

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#local-server-recommended-for-active-development)

Local Server (Recommended for Active Development)

*   Run the Auggie CLI locally as an MCP server (stdio)
*   Your client accesses `codebase-retrieval` for your working directory
*   Indexes in real-time as you edit — no manual sync required

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#remote-server-best-for-adding/understanding-code)

Remote Server (Best for Adding/Understanding Code)

*   Connect to Augment-hosted Context Engine over HTTP
*   Integrates with Augment GitHub App
*   Best for:
    *   Adding to an existing codebase
    *   Talking to / understanding the codebase
    *   Cross-repo context
    *   CI/server environments without a local working tree

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#credit-cost-for-mcp)

Credit cost for MCP

For a limited time, all users who use the Context Engine MCP in February will receive 1000 free context engine MCP tool calls.

Context Engine MCP consumes credits at different rates per query based on the underlying costs and amount of retrieval required. In our experience, we’ve seen the average per query cost between 40-70 credits per query.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#how-indexing-works)

How Indexing Works
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#local-indexing)

Local Indexing

*   Real-time indexing of your working directory
*   Picks up local file changes immediately
*   No manual sync required

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#remote-indexing)

Remote Indexing

*   Repositories connected via the Augment GitHub App are automatically indexed
*   **What’s indexed:** All selected repositories’ default branches (selected during GitHub App installation)
*   **When it updates:** Automatically when commits are pushed to the default branch

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#connect-to-mcp)

Connect to MCP
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Sign up** at [augmentcode.com](https://augmentcode.com/)
    
2.  **Get your configuration** at [app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration](https://app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration)
    

The configuration page provides ready-to-use setup instructions for your MCP client, including authentication details for both interactive (OAuth) and non-interactive (API key) use cases.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/overview#quickstart-guides)

Setup Augment

Keyboard Shortcuts for JetBrains IDEs

On this page

*   [About keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/jetbrains-keyboard-shortcuts#about-keyboard-shortcuts)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/jetbrains-keyboard-shortcuts#about-keyboard-shortcuts)

About keyboard shortcuts
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment is deeply integrated into your IDE and utilizes many of the standard keyboard shortcuts you are already familiar with. These shortcuts allow you to quickly accept suggestions, write code, and navigate your codebase. We also suggest updating a few keyboard shortcuts to make working with code suggestions even easier.

*   MacOS
    
*   Windows/Linux
    

To update keyboard shortcuts, use one of the following:

| Method | Action |
| --- | --- |
| Keyboard | Cmd , select Keymap |
| Menu bar | IntelliJ IDEA > Settings > Keymap |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/jetbrains-keyboard-shortcuts#general)

General
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Default shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Open Augment panel | Cmd Option I |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/jetbrains-keyboard-shortcuts#chat)

Chat
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Default shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Focus or open Chat panel | Cmd Option I |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/jetbrains-keyboard-shortcuts#completions)

Completions
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Default shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Accept entire suggestion | Tab |
| Accept word-by-word | Option Right |
| Reject suggestion | Esc |
| Toggle automatic completions | Cmd Option 9 |

To update keyboard shortcuts, use one of the following:

| Method | Action |
| --- | --- |
| Keyboard | Ctrl , then select Keymap |
| Menu bar | File > Settings > Keymap |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/jetbrains-keyboard-shortcuts#general-2)

General
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Default shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Open Augment panel | Ctrl Alt I |

# Completions - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/completions#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Completions

On this page

*   [About Code Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/completions#about-code-completions)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/completions#about-code-completions)

About Code Completions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment’s Code Completions integrates with your IDE’s native completions system to give you autocomplete-like suggestions as you type. You can accept all of a suggestion, accept partial suggestions a word or a line at a time, or just keep typing to ignore the suggestion.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/completions#using-code-completions)

Using Code Completions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use code completions, simply start typing in your IDE. Augment will provide suggestions based on the context of your code. You can accept a suggestion by pressing Tab, or ignore it by continuing to type. For example, add the following function to a TypeScript file:

Copy

Ask AI

    function getUser(): Promise<User>;
    

As you type `getUser`, Augment will suggest the function signature. Press Tab to accept the suggestion. Augment will continue to offer suggestions until the function is complete, at which point you will have a function similar to:

Copy

Ask AI

    function getUser(): Promise<User> {
      return fetch("/api/user/1")
        .then((response) => response.json())
        .then((json) => {
          return json as User;
        });
    }
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/completions#accepting-completions)

Accepting Completions

*   MacOS
    
*   Windows/Linux
    

We recommend configuring a custom keybinding to accept a word or line, see [Keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts)
 for more details.

| Action | Default keyboard shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Accept inline suggestion | Tab |
| Accept next word of suggestion | Cmd → |
| Accept next line of suggestion | None (see above) |
| Reject suggestion | Esc |
| Ignore suggestion | Continue typing through the suggestion |
| Toggle automatic completions | VSCode: Cmd Option A |
|     | JetBrains: Cmd Option 9 |

We recommend configuring a custom keybinding to accept a word or line, see [Keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts)
 for more details.

| Action | Default keyboard shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Accept inline suggestion | Tab |
| Accept next word of suggestion | Ctrl → |
| Accept next line of suggestion | None (see above) |
| Reject suggestion | Esc |
| Ignore suggestion | Continue typing through the suggestion |
| Toggle automatic completions | VSCode: Ctrl Alt A |
|     | JetBrains: Ctrl Alt 9 |

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/completions#disabling-completions)

Disabling Completions

*   Visual Studio Code
    
*   JetBrains IDEs
    

You can disable automatic code completions by clicking the overflow menu icon

at the top-right of the Augment panel, then selecting Turn Automatic Completions Off.

You can disable automatic code completions by clicking the Augment icon ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-smile.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=a39dac81c0ae990b2c8143421f4144c5) in the status bar at the bottom right corner of your IDE, then selecting Disable Completions.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/completions#enable-completions)

Enable Completions

*   Visual Studio Code
    
*   JetBrains IDEs
    

If you’ve temporarily disabled completions, you can re-enable them by clicking the overflow menu icon

at the top-right of the Augment panel, then selecting Turn Automatic Completions On.

If you’ve temporarily disabled completions, you can re-enable them by clicking the Augment icon ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-smile.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=a39dac81c0ae990b2c8143421f4144c5) in the status bar at the bottom right corner of your IDE, then selecting Enable Completions.

[Example Prompts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts)

Setup Augment

Install Augment for JetBrains IDEs

On this page

*   [About Installation](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#about-installation)
    
*   [Installing Augment for JetBrains IDEs](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#installing-augment-for-jetbrains-ides)
    
*   [Installing Beta versions of Augment for JetBrains IDEs](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#installing-beta-versions-of-augment-for-jetbrains-ides)
    

Augment requires version `2024.3` or above for all JetBrains IDEs. [See JetBrains documentation](https://www.jetbrains.com/help/)
 on how to update your IDE.

[Get the Augment Plugin\
----------------------\
\
Install Augment for JetBrains IDEs](https://plugins.jetbrains.com/plugin/24072-augment)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#about-installation)

About Installation
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Installing [Augment for JetBrains IDEs](https://plugins.jetbrains.com/plugin/24072-augment)
 is easy and will take you less than a minute. Augment is compatible with all JetBrains IDEs, including WebStorm, PyCharm, and IntelliJ. You can find the Augment plugin in the JetBrains Marketplace and install it following the instructions below. ![Augment plugin in JetBrains Marketplace](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/jetbrains-plugin.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=9039fe18ab88f1df9ddb047a7da9518c)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#installing-augment-for-jetbrains-ides)

Installing Augment for JetBrains IDEs
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For these instructions we’ll use _JetBrains IntelliJ_ as an example, anywhere you see _IntelliJ_ replace the name of the JetBrains IDE you’re using.In the case of Android Studio, which is based on IntelliJ, please ensure that your installation uses a runtime with JCEF. Go to Help > Find Action, type Choose Boot Java Runtime for the IDE and press Enter. Ensure the current runtime ends with `-jcef`; if not, select one **with JCEF** from the options below.

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#)

Make sure you have the latest version of your IDE installed

You can download the latest version of JetBrains IDEs from the [JetBrains](https://www.jetbrains.com/ides/#choose-your-ide)
 website. If you already have IntelliJ installed, you can update to the latest version by going to IntelliJ IDEA > Check for Updates....

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#)

Open the Plugins settings in your IDE

From the menu bar, go to IntelliJ IDEA > Settings..., or use the keyboard shortcut Cmd/Ctrl , to open the Settings window. Select Plugins from the sidebar.

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#)

Search for Augment in the marketplace

Using the search bar in the Plugins panel, search for Augment.

4

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#)

Install the extension

Click Install to install the extension. Then click OK to close the Settings window.

5

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#)

Sign into Augment and get coding

Sign in to by clicking Sign in to Augment in the Augment panel. If you do not see the Augment panel, use the shortcut Cmd/Ctrl L or click the Augment icon ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-simple.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=549509ac3a1fbdeb2700fb4b9f8f03ad) in the side bar of your IDE. See more details in [Sign In](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in)
.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#installing-beta-versions-of-augment-for-jetbrains-ides)

Installing Beta versions of Augment for JetBrains IDEs
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to get a specific bug fix or feature, sometimes you may need to _temporarily_ install a beta version of Augment for JetBrains IDEs. To do this, follow the steps below:

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#)

Download an archive of the beta version

You can download the latest beta version of Augment from [JetBrains Marketplace](https://plugins.jetbrains.com/plugin/24072-augment/versions/beta?noRedirect=true)
 website. Please click Download on the latest version and save the archive to disk.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#)

Open the Plugins settings in your IDE

From the menu bar, go to IntelliJ IDEA > Settings..., or use the keyboard shortcut Cmd/Ctrl , to open the Settings window. Select Plugins from the sidebar.

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides#)

Install Augment from the downloaded archive

Click on the gear icon next to Installed tab and click Install plugin from disk.... Select the archive you downloaded in the previous step and click OK.

[Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions)
[Keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/jetbrains-keyboard-shortcuts)

⌘I

# Network configuration - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Configuration

Network configuration

On this page

*   [Network access requirements](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#network-access-requirements)
    
*   [Specific domains](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#specific-domains)
    
*   [Core production services](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#core-production-services)
    
*   [Analytics and CDN](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#analytics-and-cdn)
    
*   [Verifying connectivity](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#verifying-connectivity)
    
*   [Related resources](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#related-resources)
    

Enterprise environments with firewalls, proxy servers, or web security tools (such as Zscaler) may need to allow-list specific Augment Code URLs so the IDE extension, Auggie CLI, and Intent can connect to Augment services.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#network-access-requirements)

Network access requirements
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment Code products need access to the following URLs:

Copy

Ask AI

    *.augmentcode.com
    

**Wildcard allow-listing is the simplest and recommended approach.** This ensures all Augment services work without additional configuration as new subdomains are added.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#specific-domains)

Specific domains
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For environments where wildcard allow-listing is not possible, allow-list the following specific domains.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#core-production-services)

Core production services

Required for IDE Extension, Auggie, and Intent.

| Domain | Purpose |
| --- | --- |
| `auth.augmentcode.com` | OAuth authentication |
| `{tenantprefix}.api.augmentcode.com` | Tenant API endpoint |

As a tenant admin, you can find your tenant URL by visiting [app.augmentcode.com/settings/service-accounts](https://app.augmentcode.com/settings/service-accounts)
. It follows the format `https://e5.api.augmentcode.com/`.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#analytics-and-cdn)

Analytics and CDN

| URL | Purpose |
| --- | --- |
| `https://evs.grdt.augmentcode.com` | Analytics and telemetry |
| `https://cdn.augmentcode.com` | Auto-updates |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#verifying-connectivity)

Verifying connectivity
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After configuring your firewall or proxy, verify that the allow-listing is working:

1.  Open your IDE with the Augment extension installed.
2.  Attempt to sign in to Augment Code.
3.  If authentication succeeds and the extension connects, your network configuration is correct.

If you encounter connection errors, review your firewall logs for blocked requests to the domains listed above.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration#related-resources)

Related resources
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For outbound IP allow-listing needs, see [Static IP allowlists](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/static-ip-support)
.

[Install Augment GitHub App](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-github-app)
[Install extension](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code)

# Index your workspace - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Setup Augment

Index your workspace

On this page

*   [About indexing your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#about-indexing-your-workspace)
    
*   [Security and privacy](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#security-and-privacy)
    
*   [What gets indexed](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#what-gets-indexed)
    
*   [Ignoring files with .augmentignore](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#ignoring-files-with-augmentignore)
    
*   [Including files that are .gitignored](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#including-files-that-are-gitignored)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#about-indexing-your-workspace)

About indexing your workspace
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you open a workspace with Augment enabled, your codebase will be automatically uploaded to Augment’s secure cloud. You can control what files get indexed using `.gitignore` and `.augmentignore` files. Indexing usually takes less than a minute but can take longer depending on the size of your codebase.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#security-and-privacy)

Security and privacy
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment stores your code securely and privately to enable our powerful context engine. We ensure code privacy through a proof-of-possession API and maintain strict internal data minimization principles. [Read more about our security](https://www.augmentcode.com/security)
.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#what-gets-indexed)

What gets indexed
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment will index all the files in your workspace, except for the files that match patterns in your `.gitignore` file and the `.augmentignore` file.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#ignoring-files-with-augmentignore)

Ignoring files with .augmentignore
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `.augmentignore` file is a list of file patterns that Augment will ignore when indexing your workspace. Create an `.augmentignore` file in the root of your workspace. You can use any glob pattern that is supported by the [gitignore](https://git-scm.com/docs/gitignore)
 file.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#including-files-that-are-gitignored)

Including files that are .gitignored
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have a file or directory in your `.gitignore` that you want to indexed, you can add it to your `.augmentignore` file using the `!` prefix. For example, you may want your `node_modules` indexed to provide Augment with context about the dependencies in their project, but it is typically included in their `.gitignore`. Add `!node_modules` to your `.augmentignore` file.

.augmentignore

.gitignore

Copy

Ask AI

    # Include .gitignore excluded files with ! prefix
    !node_modules
    
    # Exclude other files with .gitignore syntax
    data/test.json
    

[Keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/jetbrains-keyboard-shortcuts)
[Using Agent](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent)

# Setup Model Context Protocol servers - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/mcp#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Agent

Setup Model Context Protocol servers

On this page

*   [About Model Context Protocol servers](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/mcp#about-model-context-protocol-servers)
