Setup Augment

Install Augment for Visual Studio Code

On this page

*   [About Installation](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#about-installation)
    
*   [Installing Augment for Visual Studio Code](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#installing-augment-for-visual-studio-code)
    
*   [About pre-release versions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#about-pre-release-versions)
    

[Get the Augment Extension\
-------------------------\
\
Install Augment for Visual Studio Code](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=augment.vscode-augment)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#about-installation)

About Installation
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Installing [Augment for Visual Studio Code](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=augment.vscode-augment)
 is easy and will take you less than a minute. You can install the extension directly from the Visual Studio Code Marketplace or follow the instructions below. ![Augment extension in Visual Studio Code Marketplace](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu/images/vscode-extension.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu&q=85&s=12f768ba87c8887c995c615956d86e29)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#installing-augment-for-visual-studio-code)

Installing Augment for Visual Studio Code
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#)

Make sure you have the latest version of Visual Studio Code installed

You can download the latest version of Visual Studio Code from the [Visual Studio Code website](https://code.visualstudio.com/)
. If you already have Visual Studio Code installed, you can update to the latest version by going to Code > Check for Updates....

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#)

Open the Extensions panel in Visual Studio Code

Click the Extensions icon in the sidebar to show the Extensions panel.

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#)

Search for Augment in the marketplace

Using the search bar in the Extensions panel, search for Augment.

4

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#)

Install the extension

Click Install to install the extension.

5

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#)

Sign into Augment and get coding

Sign in to by clicking Sign in to Augment in the Augment panel. If you do not see the Augment panel, use the shortcut Cmd/Ctrl L or click the Augment icon ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-simple.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=549509ac3a1fbdeb2700fb4b9f8f03ad) in the side bar of your IDE. See more details in [Sign In](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in)
.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code#about-pre-release-versions)

About pre-release versions
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We regularly publish pre-release versions of the Augment extension. To use the pre-release version, go to the Augment extension in the Extensions panel and click Switch to Pre-Release Version and then Restart extensions. Pre-release versions may sometimes contain bugs or otherwise be unstable. As with the released version, please report any problems by sending us [feedback](https://docs.augmentcode.com/troubleshooting/feedback)
.

[Network configuration](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/network-configuration)
[Sign in and out](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in)

⌘I

# Droid Quickstart - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-droid#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Context Engine MCP

Droid Quickstart

*   Local Server
    
*   Remote Server
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-droid#1-install-auggie-cli)

1\. Install Auggie CLI

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install -g @augmentcode/auggie@latest
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-droid#2-sign-in-to-augment)

2\. Sign in to Augment

Copy

Ask AI

    auggie login
    

This will open a browser window for authentication.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-droid#3-configure-the-mcp-server-in-droid)

3\. Configure the MCP server in Droid

Add the Augment Context Engine MCP server:

Copy

Ask AI

    droid mcp add augment-code "auggie" --mcp --mcp-auto-workspace
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-droid#4-test-the-integration)

4\. Test the integration

Copy

Ask AI

    Prompt: "Do you have access to the Augment codebase retrieval tool?"
    

Droid should confirm it has access to the `codebase-retrieval` tool.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-droid#advanced-non-interactive-setup)

Advanced: Non-Interactive Setup
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For non-interactive environments like CI/CD pipelines, GitHub Actions, or automated scripts where you cannot run `auggie login` interactively, you can configure authentication using environment variables.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-droid#1-get-your-authentication-token)

1\. Get your authentication token

Copy

Ask AI

    auggie token print
    

This will output something like:

Copy

Ask AI

    TOKEN={"accessToken":"your-access-token","tenantURL":"your-tenant-url","scopes":["read","write"]}
    

Copy the `accessToken` value (the long string after `"accessToken":"`) and the `tenantURL` value.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-droid#2-configure-with-environment-variables)

2\. Configure with environment variables

Copy

Ask AI

    droid mcp add augment-code "auggie" --mcp --mcp-auto-workspace --env AUGMENT_API_TOKEN=your-access-token --env AUGMENT_API_URL=your-tenant-url
    

Replace `your-access-token` and `your-tenant-url` with the values from step 1.

1.  Sign up at [augmentcode.com](https://augmentcode.com/)
    
2.  Follow the setup instructions at [app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration](https://app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration)
    

[Zed Quickstart](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-zed)
[Quickstart](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview)

⌘I

# Index your workspace - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Setup Augment

Index your workspace

On this page

*   [About indexing your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#about-indexing-your-workspace)
    
*   [Security and privacy](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#security-and-privacy)
    
*   [What gets indexed](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#what-gets-indexed)
    
*   [Ignoring files with .augmentignore](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#ignoring-files-with-augmentignore)
    
*   [Including files that are .gitignored](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#including-files-that-are-gitignored)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#about-indexing-your-workspace)

About indexing your workspace
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you open a workspace with Augment enabled, your codebase will be automatically uploaded to Augment’s secure cloud. You can control what files get indexed using `.gitignore` and `.augmentignore` files. Indexing usually takes less than a minute but can take longer depending on the size of your codebase. In Visual Studio Code, you can use Workspace Context to [view what files are indexed](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#view-index-status-in-visual-studio-code)
 and [add additional context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#add-context-to-your-workspace)
.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#security-and-privacy)

Security and privacy
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment stores your code securely and privately to enable our powerful context engine. We ensure code privacy through a proof-of-possession API and maintain strict internal data minimization principles. [Read more about our security](https://www.augmentcode.com/security)
.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#what-gets-indexed)

What gets indexed
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment will index all the files in your workspace, except for the files that match patterns in your `.gitignore` file and the `.augmentignore` file. You can [view what files are indexed](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#view-sync-status-in-visual-studio-code)
 in Workspace Context.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#ignoring-files-with-augmentignore)

Ignoring files with .augmentignore
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `.augmentignore` file is a list of file patterns that Augment will ignore when indexing your workspace. Create an `.augmentignore` file in the root of your workspace. You can use any glob pattern that is supported by the [gitignore](https://git-scm.com/docs/gitignore)
 file.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#including-files-that-are-gitignored)

Including files that are .gitignored
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have a file or directory in your `.gitignore` that you want to indexed, you can add it to your `.augmentignore` file using the `!` prefix. For example, you may want your `node_modules` indexed to provide Augment with context about the dependencies in their project, but it is typically included in their `.gitignore`. Add `!node_modules` to your `.augmentignore` file.

.augmentignore

.gitignore

Copy

Ask AI

    # Include .gitignore excluded files with ! prefix
    !node_modules
    
    # Exclude other files with .gitignore syntax
    data/test.json
    

[Keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts)
[Adding additional context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode)

⌘I

# Using Actions in Chat - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-actions#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Chat

Using Actions in Chat

On this page

*   [Using actions in Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-actions#using-actions-in-chat)
    

![Augment Chat Actions](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/chat-actions.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=7e28137d1682a5b7c5d6376870b92a59)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-actions#using-actions-in-chat)

Using actions in Chat
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use a quick action, you an use a / command or click the up arrow icon

to show the available actions. For explain, fix, and test actions, first highlight the code in the editor and then use the command.

| Action | Usage |
| --- | --- |
| /find | Use natural language to find code or functionality |
| /explain | Augment will explain the hightlighted code |
| /fix | Augment will suggest improvements or find errors in the highlighted code |
| /test | Augment will suggest tests for the highlighted code |

Augment will typically include code blocks in the response to the action. See [Applying code blocks from Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-apply)
 for more details.

[Code Blocks](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-apply)
[Example Prompts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-prompts)

⌘I

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#about-chatting-with-your-codebase)

About chatting with your codebase
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment’s Chat has deep understanding about your codebase, dependencies, and best practices. You can use Chat to ask questions about your code, but it also can help you with general software engineering questions, think through technical decisions, explore new libraries, and more.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#enhancing-your-prompt)

Enhancing your prompt
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can improve the quality of your by starting with a well crafted prompt. You can start with a quick or incomplete prompt and use the prompt enhancer to add relevant references, structure, and conventions from your codebase to improve the prompt before it is sent.

1.  Write your prompt in the prompt input box
2.  Click the Enhance Prompt ✨ button
3.  Review and edit the enhanced prompt
4.  Submit your prompt

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#example-prompts)

Example Prompts
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#explain-code)

Explain code

*   Explain this codebase to me
*   How do I use the Twilio API to send a text message?
*   Explain how generics work in TypeScript and give me a simple example

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#finding-code)

Finding code

*   Where are all the useEffect hooks that depend on the ‘currentUser’ variable?
*   Find the decorators that implement retry logic across our microservices
*   Find coroutines that handle database transactions without a timeout parameter

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#generate-code)

Generate code

*   Write a function to check if a string is a valid email address
*   Generate a middleware function that rate-limits API requests using a sliding window algorithm
*   Create a SQL query to find the top 5 customers who spent the most money last month

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#write-tests)

Write tests

*   Write integration tests for this API endpoint
*   What edge cases have I not included in this test?
*   Generate mock data for testing this customer order processing function

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#refactor-and-improve-code)

Refactor and improve code

*   This function is running slowly with large collections - how can I optimize it?
*   Refactor this callback-based code to use async/await instead
*   Rewrite this function in Rust

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-prompts#find-and-fix-errors)

Find and fix errors

*   This endpoint sometimes returns a 500 error. Here’s the error log - what’s wrong?
*   I’m getting ‘TypeError: Cannot read property ‘length’ of undefined’ in this component.
*   Getting CORS errors when my frontend tries to fetch from the API

[Quick Actions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-actions)
[Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/completions)

On this page

*   [About Authentication](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#about-authentication)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#about-authentication)

About Authentication
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can sign in to Augment using one of the supported identity providers–Google or Microsoft–or sign in using your email address and a single-use code we send to you. During the process, you will be redirected to your browser to sign in to your account.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#sign-in)

Sign in
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#)

Sign in to Augment

Click the Sign in to Augment button in the Augment panel. If you do not see the Augment panel press Cmd/Ctrl L. If you are using Visual Studio Code, you be asked to confirm going to Augment’s authentication portal.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#)

Sign in with your email

In your browser, you may sign in with Google, Microsoft, or by receiving a single-use code in your email.

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#)

Accept the terms and conditions

If this is the first time you’ve signed in to Augment, you will be asked to accept the terms and conditions.

4

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#)

Return to your IDE

You will be automically redirected back to your IDE and you will see the Augment icon change to ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-smile.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=a39dac81c0ae990b2c8143421f4144c5) in the status bar.

5

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#)

Sync your workspace

If this is your first time using Augment, or you are working on a new workspace, you will see the Sync modal in the Augment panel. Click the Sync button in the Augment panel to enable Augment’s rich codebase awareness. See [Syncing your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing)
 to customize syncing behavior and learn more.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#sign-out)

Sign out
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#)

Show the Augment command menu

Press Cmd/Ctrl Shift A to show the Augment command menu.

2

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#)

Click Sign Out

Click Sign Out from the bottom of the commands menu.

3

[](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/sign-in#)

You are now signed out of Augment

You will see the status bar icon change to orange and you will be signed out of Augment in all of your active workspaces.

[Install extension](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/install-visual-studio-code)
[Keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts)

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-apply#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Chat

Applying code blocks from Chat

On this page

*   [Using code blocks from within Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-apply#using-code-blocks-from-within-chat)
    

![Augment Chat Apply](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/chat-apply.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=2e3a50fd918339cb519553c06bc5a242)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-apply#using-code-blocks-from-within-chat)

Using code blocks from within Chat
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Whenever Chat responds with code, you will have the option to add the code to your codebase. The most common option will be shown as a button and you can access the other options by clicking the overflow menu icon

at the top-right of the code block. You can use the following options to apply the code:

*   **Copy** the code from the block to your clipboard
*   **Create** a new file with the code from the block
*   **Apply** the code from the block intelligently to your file

[Focusing Context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-context)
[Quick Actions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-actions)

⌘I

*   [Direct Context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview#direct-context)
    
*   [FileSystem Context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview#filesystem-context)
    
*   [Next Steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview#next-steps)
    

**Experimental API** - Context Engine SDK is experimental and subject to breaking changes.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview#installation)

Installation
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install -g @augmentcode/auggie@latest && npm install @augmentcode/auggie-sdk
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview#getting-credentials)

Getting Credentials
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sign in to Augment using the CLI:

Copy

Ask AI

    auggie login
    

Your credentials will be stored in `~/.augment/session.json` and the SDK will automatically use them. Alternatively, you can use environment variables:

Copy

Ask AI

    export AUGMENT_API_TOKEN="your-api-token"
    export AUGMENT_API_URL="https://your-tenant.api.augmentcode.com"
    

**Finding your tenant URL:** After signing in with `auggie login`, run `auggie token print` to see your API token and tenant URL. The URL format is `https://[your-organization-name].api.augmentcode.com`.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview#direct-context)

Direct Context
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Explicitly index files from any source (APIs, databases, memory, disk) with full control over what gets indexed and the ability to save/load state:

TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { DirectContext } from '@augmentcode/auggie-sdk';
    
    async function main() {
      // Authentication is automatic via:
      // 1. Options parameters (apiKey, apiUrl passed to create())
      // 2. Environment variables (AUGMENT_API_TOKEN, AUGMENT_API_URL)
      // 3. ~/.augment/session.json (created by `auggie login`)
      const context = await DirectContext.create();
    
      // Add files to index
      const result = await context.addToIndex([\
        { path: 'src/main.ts', contents: 'export function main() { ... }' },\
        { path: 'src/auth.ts', contents: 'export function authenticate() { ... }' }\
      ]);
    
      console.log(`Newly uploaded: ${result.newlyUploaded.length}`);
      console.log(`Already uploaded: ${result.alreadyUploaded.length}`);
    
      // Search - returns formatted string ready for LLM use or display
      const results = await context.search('authentication logic');
      console.log(results);
    
      // Or use searchAndAsk for one-step Q&A
      const answer = await context.searchAndAsk(
        'How does authentication work?'
      );
      console.log(answer);
    
      // Save state to avoid re-indexing
      await context.exportToFile('/tmp/state.json');
    }
    
    main();
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview#filesystem-context)

FileSystem Context
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Automatically index and search a local directory - just point to a directory path and start searching, perfect for local development and testing:

TypeScript

Python

Copy

Ask AI

    import { FileSystemContext } from '@augmentcode/auggie-sdk';
    
    async function main() {
      const context = await FileSystemContext.create({
        directory: '/path/to/workspace',
      });
    
      // Search the directory
      const results = await context.search('authentication logic');
      console.log(results);
    
      // Or ask a question
      const answer = await context.searchAndAsk(
        'How does authentication work?'
      );
      console.log(answer);
    
      // Clean up
      await context.close();
    }
    
    main();
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/sdk/overview#next-steps)

Vim and Neovim

On this page

*   [Starting a new conversation](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/using-augment/vim-chat#starting-a-new-conversation)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/using-augment/vim-chat#using-chat)

Using chat
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Chat is a new way to work with your codebase using natural language. Use Chat to explore your codebase, quickly get up to speed on unfamiliar code, and get help working through a technical problem.

| Command | Action |
| --- | --- |
| :Augment chat <message> | Send a chat message to Augment |
| :Augment chat-new | Start a new chat conversation |
| :Augment chat-toggle | Toggle the chat panel visibility |

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/using-augment/vim-chat#sending-a-message)

Sending a message

You can send a message to Chat using the :Augment chat command. You can send your message as an optional argument to the command or enter it into the command-line when prompted. Each new message will continue the current conversation which will be used as context for your next message. **Focusing on selected text** If you have text selected in `visual mode`, Augment will automatically include it in your message. This is useful for asking questions about specific code or requesting changes to the selected code.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/using-augment/vim-chat#starting-a-new-conversation)

Starting a new conversation

You can start a new conversation by using the :Augment chat-new command.

### Next steps

*   [Using Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/using-augment/vim-completions)
    
*   [Configure keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/vim-keyboard-shortcuts)
    

[Index your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing)
[Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/using-augment/vim-completions)

# Add context to your workspace - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-context-vim#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Setup Augment

Add context to your workspace

On this page

*   [About Workspace Context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-context-vim#about-workspace-context)
    
*   [Add context to your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-context-vim#add-context-to-your-workspace)
    

Availability

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-context-vim#about-workspace-context)

About Workspace Context
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment is powered by its deep understanding of your code. You’ll need to configure your project’s source in your workspace context to get full codebase understanding in your chats and suggestions. Sometimes important parts of your system exist outside of the current project. For example, you may have seperate frontend and backend repositories or have many services across multiple repositories. Adding additional codebases to your workspace context will improve the code suggestions and chat responses from Augment.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-context-vim#add-context-to-your-workspace)

Add context to your workspace
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Be sure to set `g:augment_workspace_folders` before the Augment plugin is loaded.

To add context to your workspace, in your `.vimrc` set `g:augment_workspace_folders` to a list of paths to the folders you want to add to your workspace context. For example:

Copy

Ask AI

    let g:augment_workspace_folders = ['/path/to/folder', '~/path/to/another/folder']
    

You may want to ignore specific folders, like `node_modules`, see [Ignoring files with .augmentignore](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#ignoring-files-with-augmentignore)
 for more details. After adding a workspace folder and restarting Vim, the output of the :Augment status command will include the syncing progress for the added folder.

[Commands and shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/vim-keyboard-shortcuts)
[Index your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing)

# Codex Quickstart - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-codex#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Navigation

Context Engine MCP

Codex Quickstart

*   Local Server
    
*   Remote Server
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-codex#1-install-auggie-cli)

1\. Install Auggie CLI

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install -g @augmentcode/auggie@latest
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-codex#2-sign-in-to-augment)

2\. Sign in to Augment

Copy

Ask AI

    auggie login
    

This will open a browser window for authentication.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-codex#3-configure-the-mcp-server-in-codex)

3\. Configure the MCP server in Codex

Add the MCP server using the Codex CLI:

Copy

Ask AI

    codex mcp add codebase-retrieval -- auggie --mcp --mcp-auto-workspace
    

The `--mcp-auto-workspace` flag automatically detects your workspace when using Codex.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-codex#4-test-the-integration)

4\. Test the integration

Run Codex and prompt it with:

Copy

Ask AI

    "What is this project? Please use the codebase-retrieval tool to get the answer."
    

Codex should confirm it has access to the `codebase-retrieval` tool.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-codex#advanced-non-interactive-setup)

Advanced: Non-Interactive Setup
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For non-interactive environments like CI/CD pipelines, GitHub Actions, or automated scripts where you cannot run `auggie login` interactively, you can configure authentication using environment variables.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-codex#1-get-your-authentication-token)

1\. Get your authentication token

Copy

Ask AI

    auggie token print
    

This will output something like:

Copy

Ask AI

    TOKEN={"accessToken":"your-access-token","tenantURL":"your-tenant-url","scopes":["read","write"]}
    

Copy the `accessToken` value (the long string after `"accessToken":"`) and the `tenantURL` value.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-codex#2-configure-with-environment-variables)

2\. Configure with environment variables

Copy

Ask AI

    codex mcp add codebase-retrieval --env AUGMENT_API_TOKEN=your-access-token --env AUGMENT_API_URL=your-tenant-url -- auggie --mcp --mcp-auto-workspace
    

Replace `your-access-token` and `your-tenant-url` with the values from step 1.

1.  Sign up at [augmentcode.com](https://augmentcode.com/)
    
2.  Follow the setup instructions at [app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration](https://app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration)
    

[Claude Code Quickstart](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-claude-code)
[Kilo Quickstart](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-kilo)

Claude Code Quickstart

*   Local Server
    
*   Remote Server
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-claude-code#1-install-auggie-cli)

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install -g @augmentcode/auggie@latest

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-claude-code#2-sign-in-to-augment)

Copy

Ask AI

    auggie login
    

This will open a browser window for authentication.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-claude-code#3-configure-the-mcp-server-in-claude-code)

3\. Configure the MCP server in Claude Code

Add the MCP server to user scope (available in all projects):

Copy

Ask AI

    claude mcp add-json auggie --scope user '{"type":"stdio","command":"auggie","args":["--mcp","--mcp-auto-workspace"]}'
    

Or add to project scope (only available in the current project):

Copy

Ask AI

    claude mcp add-json auggie --scope project '{"type":"stdio","command":"auggie","args":["--mcp","--mcp-auto-workspace"]}'

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-claude-code#4-test-the-integration)

Copy

Ask AI

    claude --print "Do you have access to the Augment codebase retrieval tool? Answer in one sentence."
    

Claude should confirm it has access to the `codebase-retrieval` tool.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-claude-code#advanced-non-interactive-setup)

Advanced: Non-Interactive Setup
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For non-interactive environments like CI/CD pipelines, GitHub Actions, or automated scripts where you cannot run `auggie login` interactively, you can configure authentication using environment variables.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-claude-code#1-get-your-authentication-token)

1\. Get your authentication token

Copy

Ask AI

    auggie token print
    

This will output something like:

Copy

Ask AI

    TOKEN={"accessToken":"your-access-token","tenantURL":"your-tenant-url","scopes":["read","write"]}
    

Copy the `accessToken` value (the long string after `"accessToken":"`) and the `tenantURL` value.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-claude-code#2-configure-with-environment-variables)

2\. Configure with environment variables

Copy

Ask AI

    claude mcp add-json auggie --scope user '{"type":"stdio","command":"auggie","args":["--mcp","--mcp-auto-workspace"],"env":{"AUGMENT_API_TOKEN":"your-access-token","AUGMENT_API_URL":"your-tenant-url"}}'
    

Replace `your-access-token` and `your-tenant-url` with the values from step 1.

1.  Sign up at [augmentcode.com](https://augmentcode.com/)
    
2.  Follow the setup instructions at [app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration](https://app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration)

# Completions - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Navigation

Visual Studio Code

Completions

On this page

*   [About Code Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#about-code-completions)
    
*   [Using Code Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#using-code-completions)
    
*   [Accepting Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#accepting-completions)
    
*   [Disabling Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#disabling-completions)
    
*   [Enable Completions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#enable-completions)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#about-code-completions)

About Code Completions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment’s Code Completions integrates with your IDE’s native completions system to give you autocomplete-like suggestions as you type. You can accept all of a suggestion, accept partial suggestions a word or a line at a time, or just keep typing to ignore the suggestion.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#using-code-completions)

Using Code Completions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use code completions, simply start typing in your IDE. Augment will provide suggestions based on the context of your code. You can accept a suggestion by pressing Cmd/Ctrl →, or ignore it by continuing to type. For example, add the following function to a TypeScript file:

Copy

Ask AI

    function getUser(): Promise<User>;
    

As you type `getUser`, Augment will suggest the function signature. Press Tab to accept the suggestion. Augment will continue to offer suggestions until the function is complete, at which point you will have a function similar to:

Copy

Ask AI

    function getUser(): Promise<User> {
      return fetch("/api/user/1")
        .then((response) => response.json())
        .then((json) => {
          return json as User;
        });
    }
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#accepting-completions)

Accepting Completions

*   MacOS
    
*   Windows/Linux
    

We recommend configuring a custom keybinding to accept a word or line, see [Keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts)
 for more details.

| Action | Default keyboard shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Accept inline suggestion | Tab |
| Accept next word of suggestion | Cmd → |
| Accept next line of suggestion | None (see above) |
| Reject suggestion | Esc |
| Ignore suggestion | Continue typing through the suggestion |
| Toggle automatic completions | VSCode: Cmd Option A |
|     | JetBrains: Cmd Option 9 |

We recommend configuring a custom keybinding to accept a word or line, see [Keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts)
 for more details.

| Action | Default keyboard shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Accept inline suggestion | Tab |
| Accept next word of suggestion | Ctrl → |
| Accept next line of suggestion | None (see above) |
| Reject suggestion | Esc |
| Ignore suggestion | Continue typing through the suggestion |
| Toggle automatic completions | VSCode: Ctrl Alt A |
|     | JetBrains: Ctrl Alt 9 |

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#disabling-completions)

Disabling Completions

*   Visual Studio Code
    
*   JetBrains IDEs
    

You can disable automatic code completions by clicking the overflow menu icon

at the top-right of the Augment panel, then selecting Turn Automatic Completions Off.

You can disable automatic code completions by clicking the Augment icon ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-smile.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=a39dac81c0ae990b2c8143421f4144c5) in the status bar at the bottom right corner of your IDE, then selecting Disable Completions.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/completions#enable-completions)

Enable Completions

*   Visual Studio Code
    
*   JetBrains IDEs
    

If you’ve temporarily disabled completions, you can re-enable them by clicking the overflow menu icon

at the top-right of the Augment panel, then selecting Turn Automatic Completions On.

If you’ve temporarily disabled completions, you can re-enable them by clicking the Augment icon ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-smile.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=a39dac81c0ae990b2c8143421f4144c5) in the status bar at the bottom right corner of your IDE, then selecting Enable Completions.

[Instructions](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/instructions)
[Install extension](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/install-jetbrains-ides)

⌘I

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Setup Augment

Add context to your workspace

On this page

*   [About Workspace Context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#about-workspace-context)
    
*   [View Workspace Context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#view-workspace-context)

Availability

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#about-workspace-context)

About Workspace Context
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment is powered by its deep understanding of your code. Sometimes important parts of your system exist outside of the current workspace you have open in your IDE. For example, you may have seperate frontend and backend repositories or have many services across multiple repositories. Adding additional context to your workspace will improve the code suggestions and chat responses from Augment.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#view-workspace-context)

View Workspace Context
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To view your Workspace Context, click the folder icon in the top right corner of the Augment sidebar panel. ![Workspace Context](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu/images/workspace-context.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu&q=85&s=16e11c1644cf33c6c255cac488c0eebe)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#add-context-to-your-workspace)

Add context to your workspace
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add context to your workspace, click \+ Add more... at the bottom of the Source Folders section of the context manager. From the file browser select the folders you want to add to your workspace context and click Add Source Folder.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-context-vscode#view-sync-status)

View sync status
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When viewing Workspace Context, each file and folder will have an icon that indicates whether its sync status. The following icons indicate the sync status of each file in your workspace:

| Indicator | Status |
| --- | --- |
| ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu/images/wsc-included.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu&q=85&s=d1dd1a289906e0bc0552624154dfede1) | Synced, or sync in progress |
| ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu/images/wsc-excluded.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu&q=85&s=a811d1132ea0a90e117a9b85823ef9f6) | Not synced |
| ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu/images/wsc-partially-included.svg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=IEgTogsPIebDB-Bu&q=85&s=b311b9ab4b2c686f5ed292c9423c2744) | Some files within the folder are synced |

[Index your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/workspace-indexing)
[Using Agent](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/agent)

⌘I

Context Engine MCP

Kilo Quickstart

*   Local Server
    
*   Remote Server
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-kilo#1-install-auggie-cli)

1\. Install Auggie CLI

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install -g @augmentcode/auggie@latest
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-kilo#2-sign-in-to-augment)

2\. Sign in to Augment

Copy

Ask AI

    auggie login
    

This will open a browser window for authentication.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-kilo#3-configure-the-mcp-server-in-kilo)

3\. Configure the MCP server in Kilo

*   Click the MCP server icon ![Click the MCP server icon](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/rIravLuzI7-HsY1h/images/kilo-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rIravLuzI7-HsY1h&q=85&s=51f67b469aeeeb65d9894572289a66a0)
*   Click Edit Global MCP ![Click Edit Global MCP](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/rIravLuzI7-HsY1h/images/kilo-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rIravLuzI7-HsY1h&q=85&s=fd0d55715e4586ba29ee40cdfaf491a7)

Paste this configuration:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "augment-context-engine": {
          "command": "auggie",
          "type": "stdio",
          "args": ["--mcp", "--mcp-auto-workspace"],
          "disabled": false,
          "alwaysAllow": ["codebase-retrieval"]
        }
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/context-services/mcp/quickstart-kilo#4-test-the-integration)

Prompt: “What is this project? Please use codebase retrieval tool to get the answer.”Kilo should confirm it has access to the `codebase-retrieval` tool.![Kilo test](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/rIravLuzI7-HsY1h/images/kilo-3.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=rIravLuzI7-HsY1h&q=85&s=df1331ebf761134639118abe3736bd25)See [MCP Server Mode](https://docs.augmentcode.com/cli/reference#mcp-server-mode)
 for more options.

1.  Sign up at [augmentcode.com](https://augmentcode.com/)
    
2.  Follow the setup instructions at [app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration](https://app.augmentcode.com/mcp/configuration)

# Using Chat - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Chat

Using Chat

On this page

*   [About Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#about-chat)
    
*   [Accessing Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#accessing-chat)
    
*   [Using Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#using-chat)
    
*   [Enhancing your prompt](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#enhancing-your-prompt)
    
*   [Conversations about code](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#conversations-about-code)
    
*   [Starting a new chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#starting-a-new-chat)
    
*   [Previous chats](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#previous-chats)
    
*   [Deleting a chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#deleting-a-chat)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#about-chat)

About Chat
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Chat is a new way to work with your codebase using natural language. Chat will automatically use the current workspace as context and you can [provide focus](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-context)
 for Augment by selecting specific code blocks, files, folders, or external documentation. Details from your current chat, including the additional context, are used to provide more relevant code suggestions as well. ![Augment Chat](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/chat-explain.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=a197d0a8fe4e010828796d78d172d43e)

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#accessing-chat)

Accessing Chat
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access the Chat sidebar by clicking the Augment icon ![](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/augment-icon-chat.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=aa776a96f49e4d86cb0a0d7cef78cc67) in the sidebar or the status bar. You can also open Chat by using one of the keyboard shortcuts below. **Keyboard Shortcuts**

| Platform | Shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| MacOS | Cmd L |
| Windows/Linux | Ctrl L |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#using-chat)

Using Chat
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use Chat, simply type your question or command into the input field at the bottom of the Chat panel. You will see the currently included context which includes the workspace and current file by default. Use Chat to explain your code, investigate a bug, or use a new library. See [Example Prompts for Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat-prompts)
 for more ideas on using Chat.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#enhancing-your-prompt)

Enhancing your prompt

You can improve the quality of your by starting with a well crafted prompt. You can start with a quick or incomplete prompt and use the prompt enhancer to add relevant references, structure, and conventions from your codebase to improve the prompt before it is sent.

1.  Write your prompt in the prompt input box
2.  Click the Enhance Prompt ✨ button
3.  Review and edit the enhanced prompt
4.  Submit your prompt

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#conversations-about-code)

Conversations about code

To get the best possible results, you can go beyond asking simple questions or commands, and instead have a back and forth conversation with Chat about your code. For example, you can ask Chat to explain a specific function and then ask follow-up questions about possible refactoring options. Chat can act as a pair programmer, helping you work through a technical problem or understand unfamiliar code.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#starting-a-new-chat)

Starting a new chat

You should start a new Chat when you want to change the topic of the conversation since the current conversation is used as part of the context for your next question. To start a new chat, open the Augment panel and click the new chat icon

at the top-right of the Chat panel.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#previous-chats)

Previous chats

You can continue a chat by clicking the chevron icon

at the top-left of the Chat panel. Your previous chats will be listed in reverse chronological order, and you can continue your conversation where you left off.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat#deleting-a-chat)

Deleting a chat

You can delete a previous chat by clicking the chevron icon

at the top-left of the Chat panel to show the list of previous chats. Click the delete icon

next to the chat you want to delete. You will be asked to confirm that you want to delete the chat.

[Configure integrations](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/agent-integrations)
[Focusing Context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/chat-context)

⌘I

---

Setup Augment

Keyboard Shortcuts for Visual Studio Code

On this page

*   [About keyboard shortcuts](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts#about-keyboard-shortcuts)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts#about-keyboard-shortcuts)

About keyboard shortcuts
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment is deeply integrated into your IDE and utilizes many of the standard keyboard shortcuts you are already familiar with. These shortcuts allow you to quickly accept suggestions, write code, and navigate your codebase. We also suggest updating a few keyboard shortcuts to make working with code suggestions even easier.

*   MacOS
    
*   Windows/Linux
    

To update keyboard shortcuts, use one of the following:

| Method | Action |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Keyboard | Cmd K then Cmd S |     |
| Menu bar | Code > Settings... > Keyboard Shortcuts |     |
| Command palette | Cmd Shift P then search Preferences: Open Keyboard Shortcuts |     |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts#general)

General
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Recommended shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Open Augment panel | Cmd L |
| Show Augment commands | Cmd Shift A |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts#chat)

Chat
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Default shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Focus or open Chat panel | Cmd L |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts#next-edit)

Next Edit
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Default shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Go to next | Cmd ; |
| Go to previous | Cmd Shift ; |
| Accept suggestion | Enter |
| Reject suggestion | Backspace |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts#instructions)

Instructions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Default shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Start instruction | Cmd I |
| Accept | Return |
| Reject | Esc |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/vscode-keyboard-shortcuts#completions)

Completions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Action | Default keyboard shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Accept inline suggestion | Tab |
| Accept next word of suggestion | Cmd → |
| Accept next line of suggestion | None (see below) |
| Reject suggestion | Esc |
| Ignore suggestion | Continue typing through the suggestion |
| Toggle automatic completions | Cmd Option A |

**Recommended shortcuts**We recommend updating your keybindings to include the following shortcuts to make working with code suggestions even easier. These changes update the default behavior of Visual Studio Code.

| Action | Recommended shortcut |
| --- | --- |
| Accept next line of suggestion | Cmd Ctrl → |

To update keyboard shortcuts, use one of the following:

| --- | --- |

| Command palette | Ctrl Shift P then search Preferences: Open Keyboard Shortcuts |

*   Create a file named: opencode.json

Paste this configuration:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "$schema": "https://opencode.ai/config.json",
      "mcp": {
        "augment-context-engine": {
          "type": "local",
          "command": ["auggie", "--mcp", "--mcp-auto-workspace"],
          "enabled": true
        }
      }
    }

 for more options.

# Secrets Manager - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Agent

Secrets Manager

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#overview)
    
*   [Accessing the Secrets Manager](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#accessing-the-secrets-manager)
    
*   [Secret Types](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#secret-types)
    
*   [Environment Variables](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#environment-variables)
    
*   [Mounted Files](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#mounted-files)
    
*   [Security Features](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#security-features)
    
*   [Limits and Quotas](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#limits-and-quotas)
    
*   [Security Best Practices](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#security-best-practices)
    

Availability

The Secrets Manager allows you to securely store and manage user-defined secrets that can be used in your development environment. It supports two types of secrets: **Environment Variables** and **Mounted Files**.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#overview)

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Secrets Manager provides a secure way to store sensitive information like API keys, database credentials, and configuration secrets. All secrets are encrypted and stored securely, with automatic redaction in logs to prevent accidental exposure.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#accessing-the-secrets-manager)

Accessing the Secrets Manager
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Open the Settings Panel (gear icon in the Augment panel) and navigate to the **Secrets** section to manage your secrets.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#secret-types)

Secret Types
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#environment-variables)

Environment Variables

Environment variables are injected into your development environment and accessible via standard environment variable access patterns. **Use cases:**

*   API keys (GitHub tokens, OpenAI keys)
*   Database connection strings
*   Service endpoints
*   Configuration flags

**How they work:**

*   Secrets are made available as environment variables in your workspace
*   Generated profile script at `/etc/profile.d/15-augment-secrets.sh`
*   Automatically loaded in shell sessions

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#mounted-files)

Mounted Files

Mounted files are stored as actual files in your workspace filesystem at specified paths. **Use cases:**

*   SSH private keys
*   Certificate files
*   Configuration files
*   Large secret content

**How they work:**

*   Files are mounted to `/run/augment_secrets/` by default
*   You specify the mount path when creating the secret
*   Files are accessible via standard filesystem operations

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#security-features)

Security Features
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Secret values are never displayed by default
*   All secret values are redacted in logs
*   Each user can only access their own secrets

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#limits-and-quotas)

Limits and Quotas
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Limit | Default Value |
| --- | --- |
| Max secrets per user | 100 |
| Max secret size | 4KB |
| Max name length | 255 characters |
| Max tags per secret | 50  |

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/user-secrets#security-best-practices)

Security Best Practices
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Use descriptive names**: Make secret purposes clear without exposing sensitive info
2.  **Regular cleanup**: Remove unused secrets to minimize exposure
3.  **Avoid logging values**: The system automatically redacts secrets in logs
4.  **Use appropriate type**: Choose environment variables for simple values, mounted files for complex content

[Static IP allowlists](https://docs.augmentcode.com/setup-augment/static-ip-support)
[Using Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/using-augment/chat)

⌘I

---

# Using Agent - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

⌘KAsk AI

Agent

Using Agent

On this page

*   [About Agent](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#about-agent)
    
*   [Accessing Agent](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#accessing-agent)
    
*   [Choosing a model](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#choosing-a-model)

*   [Checkpoints](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#checkpoints)

*   [Next steps](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#next-steps)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#about-agent)

About Agent
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment Agent is a powerful tool that can help you complete software development tasks end-to-end. From quick edits to complete feature implementation, Agent breaks down your requests into a functional plan and implements each step all while keeping you informed about what actions and changes are happening. Powered by Augment’s Context Engine and powerful LLM architecture, Agent can write, document, and test like an experienced member of your team.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#accessing-agent)

Accessing Agent
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To access Agent, simply open the Augment panel and select one of the Agent modes from the drop down in the input box. ![Augment Agent](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/agent-selector-jetbrains.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=ba4dc039488f3c0a3a5ff299bd5694c2)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#choosing-a-model)

Choosing a model

Use the model dropdown in the Augment panel to switch between Claude Sonnet 4 and GPT-5. Your selection applies only to Agent for the current workspace and can be changed at any time. See [Available Models](https://docs.augmentcode.com/models/available-models)
 for details.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#using-agent)

Using Agent
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use Agent, simply type your request into the input box using natural language and click the submit button. You will see the default context including current workspace, current file, and Agent memories. You can add additional context by clicking

and selecting files or folder, or add an image as context by clicking the paperclip. Agent can create, edit, or delete code across your workspace and can use tools like the terminal and external integrations through MCP to complete your request.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#enhancing-your-prompt)

Enhancing your prompt

You can improve the quality of your by starting with a well crafted prompt. You can start with a quick or incomplete prompt and use the prompt enhancer to add relevant references, structure, and conventions from your codebase to improve the prompt before it is sent.

1.  Write your prompt in the prompt input box
2.  Click the Enhance Prompt ✨ button
3.  Review and edit the enhanced prompt
4.  Submit your prompt

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#reviewing-changes)

Reviewing changes

You can review every change Agent makes by clicking on the action to expand the view. Review diffs for file changes, see complete terminal commands and output, and the results of external integration calls. ![Augment Agent](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/agent-expand-jetbrains.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=344f87684aa38da595509b25a5139f24)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#checkpoints)

Checkpoints

Checkpoints are automatically saved snapshots of your workspace as Agent implements the plan allowing you to easily revert back to a previous step. This enables Agent to continue working while you review code changes and commands results. To revert to a previous checkpoint, click the reverse arrow to restore your code. ![Augment Agent](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/agent-checkpoint-jetbrains.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=36aa8bbceaba92de053998e158696428)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#agent-vs-agent-auto)

Agent vs Agent Auto

By default, Agent will pause work when it needs to execute a terminal command or access external integrations. After reviewing the suggested action, click the blue play button to have Agent execute the command and continue working. You tell Agent to skip a specific action by clicking on the three dots and then Skip. ![Augment Agent](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/agent-approval.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=68093b6342af74a4aa90d521b1cd2a3a) In Agent Auto, Agent will act more independently. It will edit files, execute terminal commands, and access tools like MCP servers automatically.

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#stop-or-guide-the-agent)

Stop or guide the Agent

You can interrupt the Agent at any time by clicking Stop. This will pause the action to allow you to correct something you see the agent doing incorrectly. While Agent is working, you can also prompt the Agent to try a different approach which will automatically stop the agent and prompt it to correct its course. ![Stopping the agent](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/agent-stop.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=280d36fadf5a41fa8d777be4ac1e4a96)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#quick-ask-mode)

Quick Ask Mode

Quick Ask Mode is a toggle button in the agent chat interface that restricts the AI to read-only tools only. When activated, it adds a visual badge to the message and focuses the AI on information gathering without making any changes to your codebase. ![Quick Ask Mode toggle and usage](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/ask-mode.gif?s=c2c554fd010bb15d8267de15ad4f9dc5)

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#comparison-to-chat)

Comparison to Chat

Agent takes Chat to the next level by allowing Augment to do things for you-that is create and make modifications directly to your codebase. Chat can explain code, create plans, and suggest changes which you can smartly apply one-by-one, but Agent takes it a step further by automatically implementing the entire plan and all code changes for you.

| What are you trying to do? | Chat | Agent |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Ask questions about your code | ☑️  | ✅   |
| Get advice on how to refactor code | ☑️  | ✅   |
| Add new features to selected lines of code | ☑️  | ✅   |
| Add new feature spanning multiple files |     | ✅   |
| Document new features |     | ✅   |
| Queue up tests for you in the terminal |     | ✅   |
| Open Linear tickets or start a pull request |     | ✅   |
| Start a new branch in GitHub from recent commits |     | ✅   |
| Automatically perform tasks on your behalf |     | ✅   |

### 

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#use-cases)

Use cases

Use Agent to handle various aspects of your software development workflow, from simple configuration changes to complex feature implementations. Agent supports your daily engineering tasks like:

*   **Make quick edits** - Create a pull request to adjust configuration values like feature flags from FALSE to TRUE
*   **Perform refactoring** - Move functions between files while maintaining coding conventions and ensuring bug-free operation
*   **Start a first draft for new features** - Start a pull request (PR) with implementing entirely new functionality straight from a GitHub Issue or Linear Ticket
*   **Branch from GitHub** - Open a PR from GitHub based on recent commits that creates a new branch
*   **Query Supabase tables directly** - Ask Agent to view the contents of a table
*   **Start tickets in Linear or Jira** - Open tickets and ask Agent to suggest a plan to address the ticket
*   **Add Pull Request descriptions** - Merge your PR into a branch then tell the agent to explain what the changes are and why they were made
*   **Create test coverage** - Generate unit tests for your newly developed features
*   **Generate documentation** - Produce comprehensive documentation for your libraries and features
*   **Start a README** - Write a README for a new feature or updated function that you just wrote
*   **Track development progress** - Review and summarize your recent Git commits for better visibility with the GitHub integration

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/agent#next-steps)

Next steps
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Configure Agent Integrations](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/agent-integrations)
    

[Index your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/setup-augment/workspace-indexing)
[Using Tasklist](https://docs.augmentcode.com/jetbrains/using-augment/tasklist)

# Index your workspace - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)

Setup Augment

Index your workspace

On this page

*   [About indexing your workspace](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#about-indexing-your-workspace)
    
*   [Security and privacy](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#security-and-privacy)
    
*   [What gets indexed](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#what-gets-indexed)
    
*   [Ignoring files with .augmentignore](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#ignoring-files-with-augmentignore)
    
*   [Including files that are .gitignored](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#including-files-that-are-gitignored)
    

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#about-indexing-your-workspace)

About indexing your workspace
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you open a workspace with Augment enabled, your codebase will be automatically uploaded to Augment’s secure cloud. You can control what files get indexed using `.gitignore` and `.augmentignore` files. Indexing usually takes less than a minute but can take longer depending on the size of your codebase.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#security-and-privacy)

Security and privacy
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment stores your code securely and privately to enable our powerful context engine. We ensure code privacy through a proof-of-possession API and maintain strict internal data minimization principles. [Read more about our security](https://www.augmentcode.com/security)
.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#what-gets-indexed)

What gets indexed
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Augment will index all the files in your workspace, except for the files that match patterns in your `.gitignore` file and the `.augmentignore` file.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#ignoring-files-with-augmentignore)

Ignoring files with .augmentignore
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `.augmentignore` file is a list of file patterns that Augment will ignore when indexing your workspace. Create an `.augmentignore` file in the root of your workspace. You can use any glob pattern that is supported by the [gitignore](https://git-scm.com/docs/gitignore)
 file.

[​](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-indexing#including-files-that-are-gitignored)

Including files that are .gitignored
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have a file or directory in your `.gitignore` that you want to indexed, you can add it to your `.augmentignore` file using the `!` prefix. For example, you may want your `node_modules` indexed to provide Augment with context about the dependencies in their project, but it is typically included in their `.gitignore`. Add `!node_modules` to your `.augmentignore` file.

.augmentignore

.gitignore

Copy

Ask AI

    # Include .gitignore excluded files with ! prefix
    !node_modules
    
    # Exclude other files with .gitignore syntax
    data/test.json
    

[Workspace context](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/workspace-context-vim)
[Chat](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/using-augment/vim-chat)

⌘I

# Install Augment for Vim and Neovim - Augment

[Skip to main content](https://docs.augmentcode.com/vim/setup-augment/install-vim-neovim#content-area)

[Augment home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-black.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b14be4f6a1b5677d1a8e9711b7adb0e2)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/augment-mtje7p526w/r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5/images/logo/augment-logo-white.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=r-azeXhOS4FbEUi5&q=85&s=b88ceeef88a3c84ad5f9ae2c4e774fb5)](https://docs.augmentcode.com/)
